41740739|Los rboles de la especie endmica Gyranthera caribensis Pittier fueron cartografados individualmente, desde los Estados Miranda y Vargas hasta Zulia, abarcando los lmites conocidos de su distribucin, aunque no se cont con las fotografas areas de algunas partes de Aragua y Carabobo. Se Ileg a la conclusin de que esta especie prospera en los bosques hmedos con pluviosidad mayor de 1500 mm anuales. En base a esta realidad, se pudo cartografiar la existencia de muchas reas del ecosistema. Esto es un acontecimiento de importancia para la planificacin a largo plazo para el desarrollo de Venezuela, debido a la alta diversidad biolgica involucrada y a lo impresionante de los bosques que alcanzan los 60 m de altura. Esta especie de rbol no se desarrolla en los suelos cidos de los bosques nublados; y por tal razn es indicativa del lmite inferior de dicha formacin vegetai. Adems, en las cercanas de varios pueblos y ciudades de la poca colonial, el mismo rbol se comporta corno tardo en el proceso sucesional y prospera en polgonos que representan campos de agricultura migratoria en alguna de las etapas coloniales. La Venezuela de hoy en da, debera implementar los mecanismos existentes para establecer reservas de todos los grandes bosques con esta especie. The individual large trees of the endemic Gyranthera caribensis Pittier were mapped to the extremes of their distribution, from the states of Miranda and Vargas to Zulia, although, in some parts, the aereal photographs needed were not available. This tree that prospers in areas with more than 1500 mm of annual rainfall, approximately; it is used here as a precise indicator of the zones of wet forest where few rainfall stations have been placed. Populations of this tree do not enter into the more acid soils of the higher elevation cloud forest, and for this reason this species is also an excellent indicator of the lower limit of this ecosystem. Also, near the towns that date from the days of the Spanish Empire, these trees are often concentrated in clearly marked rectangular patterns. This was interpreted as an indication of where this late secondary tree species took advantage of reforested areas that were initially opened by migratory agriculturalists during one of the colonial periods. The few tropical rain forests of northern Venezuela should all be included in reserves.

41740451|La familia de las Burseraceae estudiadas se presenta como muy homognea respecto a su estructura cortical. Los caracteres principales que reune esta familia son: sus canales secretores con contenido rojo, sus radios medulares finos, la formacin de fibras en el liber duro y la disposicin del mismo en forma de placas o bandas alternates; el ritidoma escamoso, el crecimiento de dilatacin muy moderado, la moderada formacin secundaria de clulas ptreas; el corcho y la felodermis delgadas, ausencia de estratificacin en la peridermis, la apariencia casual de paredes en forma de U en el suber, la ausencia de paredes en forma de herradura en la felodermis, y la presencia de clulas ptreas en la ltima. A pesar de que en casi todas las muestras estudiadas se observa muy poco crecimiento de dilatacin, la muestra D-77 hace una excepcin con relativamente mucho crecimiento de dilatacin no slo en los radios medulares, sino tambin en el floema entero. Notable es el parnquima de relleno con mucho almidn alrededor de los canales secretores que, en parte, parece proceder de divisiones periclinales de clulas que rodean los canales; posiblemente, este parnquima juega un papel especial en el almacenamiento de almidn y en su transformacin en azcar. La formacin de paredes en forma de herradura en el suber pude, tal vez, representar un indicio de mayor edad de la muestra, ya que se ha observado sobre todo en las capas mas jvenes del corcho, sea cerca del felgeno. Con respecto a la identificacin taxonmica por la estructura cortical de las muestras puede decirse que: las muestras X-157 y X-160 son idnticas, representando la misma especie (Protium decandrum). El Azucarito se distingue de X-157 y X-160 y representa otra especie. Tambin las muestras D-296 y D-298 son muy parecidas y eventualmente pertenecen a la misma especie. En cambio, las 3 muestras de Protium neglectum (D-166, D-262 y D-76) se distinguen entre s y posiblemente pertenecen a 3 diferentes especies. En resumen, la estructura cortical puede usarse hasta para la distincin de especies por diferencias sutiles de la mism The family of Burseraceae studied presents itself as very homogeneous regarding cortical structure. The principal characteristics common to the majority of samples are: secretory canals with a red exudation, small medullary rays, formation of fibers in the hard bast and its disposition in the form of alternating plates and bands; the scale-like rhutidome, a moderate dilatation growth and moderate secondary formation of stone cells; small crok and phelloderm, absence of stratification in the periderm, casual apperarance of U-shaped walls in the cork, absence of horseshoe-shaped walls in the phelloderm, and presence of stone cells in the latter. Dilatation growth is very moderate in almost all samples studied, exept in D-77 where vigorous dilatation growth not only in the medullary rays, but also in the entire phloem can be observed. Worth mentioning is the filling tissue around the secretory canals, rich in starch, which partly priginates by periclinal divisions of the surrounding parenchyma cells; possibly, it plays a certain paper in starch storage and its transformation in sugar. The formation of horseshoe-shaped cell walls in the cork may eventually be an indication of a more advanced stage of the sample, as it can be observed mostly in the youngest layers of the cork, near the phellogen. Regarding taxonomical identification of samples by their cortical structure, one can say: that the samples X-157 and X-160 are identical, representing the same species (Protium decandrum). The sample "Azucarito" is distinct from X-157 and X-160 and represents an other species. Also the samples D-296 and D-298 are alike and eventually pertain to the same species. On the other hand, the 3 samples of Protium negkctum (D-166, D-262 and D-76) are distinguished by several characters and possibly represent 3 different species. In all, the cortical structure may be used even for the distinction of species by very subtle differences.
41740667|El tubrculo radical se distingue de la raz filamentosa sobre todo por su abundante crecimiento en anchura. El xilema sufre una modificacin en cuanto se forman pocos vasos, pero mucho parnquima rico en almidn. Puesto que el xilema se diferencia poco, se conserva la ordenacin de las clulas en hileras radiales. El floema funcional es mnimo en el tubrculo y ia distincin entre parnquima floemtico regular y parnquima amilfero se pierde en etapas avanzadas, puesto que casi todas las clulas parenquimticas se llenan de almidn; este ltimo es del tipo compuesto. El sabor viene de las gotas de aceite etrico que se encuentran en casi todas las clulas parenquimticas, pero sobre todo en las clulas secretoras y en los canales secretores que se forman dentro del parnquima amilfero; este ltimo es del tipo aliforme confluente con respecto a la manera de rodear los canales y forma junto con los radios medulares una red de parnquima rico en almidn, visto en corte transversal. Los canales secretores se originan de manera esquizognea. El corcho se desarrolla en forma de "pisos" ("Etagen-kork") en culas superpuestas que se dividen periclinalmente; de esta manera puede adaptarse al crecimiento de dilatacin; se encuentra este tipo de corcho habitualmente en monocotiledneas. El tubrculo se hace entonces comestible por la abundancia de parnquima con paredes delgadas, tanto en el xilema como en el floema, y la ausencia casi completa de tejido mecnico. Las sustancias nutritivas del tubrculo son sobre todo el almidn y, en cantidad mucho menor, el aceite. The tuberous root is distinguished from the filamentous one principally by its growth in thickness. The xylem suffers a modication in so far as only few vessels form, but a high quantity of parenchyma, rich in starch. As the xylem differentiates little, the cell arrangement in the form of radial rows is maintained. The functional phloem remains very small and the distinction between regular phloem parenchyma and amyliferous parenchyma is lost in more advanced stages, as almost all parenchyma cells become filled with starch; this is of the compound type. The special flavour comes from the eteric oil in the form of small droplets which are found in almost all parenchyma cells, but first of all in the secretory cells and canals which develop within the amyliforous parenchyma; the latter surrounds the canals in a "aliform-confluent" way and, together with the medullary rays, forms a network of starchy cells, as seen in transverse section. The secretory canals originate schizogeneously as intercellular spaces in the center of (3 to) 4 cells. The cork develops in the form of stories in superposed cells which divide repeatedly periclinally; in this way, the cork is able to adapt to growth in circumference; this type of cork is otherwise characteristic of monocotyledones. The tubercle becomes edible through the development of high quantities of parenchyma with delicate walls which forms in the xylem as well as in the phloem, and by the almost complete absence of strong mechanic tissue. The nutritive substances of the tubercle are first of all starch and, in a much more reduced quantity, also oil.

41740685|En la Sierra Nevada de Mrida, entre los 3.000 - 4.000 m snm, crecen tres especies de Miconia (Melastomataceae): M. chionophylla, M. latifolia y M. tinifolia. La primera es un arbusto enano de los bosques de Polylepis sericea y las dos ltimas son rboles del bosque paramero. Con el objeto de describir y comparar en estas especies sus patrones de distribucin y su hbitat, se realizaron estudios morfoanatmicos foliares, colectando material de diferentes individuos a lo largo del gradiente altitudinal. Miconia latifolia y M. tinifolia ascienden hasta los 3.500 m y presentan hojas tpicamente xeromrficas: venacin reticulada, cutcula gruesa, densidad estomtica alta, epidermis de clulas pequeas, hipodermis pluriestratificada y mesofilo muy compacto. M. chionophylla, en cambio, presenta hojas mesomrficas: venacin y mesofilo laxo, cutcula delgada, densidad estomtica baja, clulas epidrmicas grandes y carece de hipodermis, pero asciende a 4.000 m snm. In the Sierra Nevada National Park, in Mrida, three species of Miconia (Melastomataceae) occur between 3.000 and 4.000 m asl. These species are: M. chionophylla, M. latifolia and M. tinifolia. The first is a dwarf shrub of the Polylepis sericea forests, whilst the other two species are trees of the upper montane forests. With the purpose of describing and comparing these three species, their distribution and habitat, the morphoanatomical characters of the leaves were studied in samples collected from individuals growing at different altitudes, along this gradient. Miconia latifolia and M. tinifolia reach 3.500 m and exhibit typical xeromorphic leaves: reticulated vein pattern, thick cuticles, elevated stomatal density, small epidermic cells, multistratified hypodermis and a compact mesophyll. M. chionophylla, instead, exhibits typical mesomorphic leaves, characterized by a lax vein pattern and mesophyll, thin cuticles, relatively low stomatal density and lacks a hypodermis, yet reaches 4.000 m asl.

41740853|Para determinar su grado de halofitismo se analiz la composicin mineral y de istopos estables (C y N) de 18 especies de plantas de comunidades costeras, y de los suelos asociados en tres localidades del estado Falcn, Venezuela, en la carretera Coro-La Vela (COVE); y la costa oriental (COP) y la baha de Tacuato (TAC), ambas en Paraguan. Los suelos de COP presentaron textura arenosa y valores menores de N, P, K y Na. Los suelos de TAC mostraron mayor salinidad (Na, Mg y Ca) y los de COVE tenan concentraciones mayores de Ny P, y textura arcillosa. Las especies de COP tenan las mayores concentraciones de Na, y eran ms suculentas (Sesuvium portulacastrum, S. edmondstonii, Batis maritima, Sarcocornia perennis y Heterostachys ritteriana). Chamaesyce mesembrianthemifolia y Croton punctatus tenan cocientes K/Na > 1 (no halfitas). Chamaesyce mesembrianthemifolia, Scaevolaplumieri, Argusia gnaphalodes, Egletesprostrata, Suriana martima y Gomphrena albiflora son concentradoras relativas de K. Las especies calcifobas acumulan la mayor parte del Ca como oxalato insoluble (Atriplex oestophora, G. albiflora y Alternanthera halimifolia), o secuestrado como fosfatos y pectatos (Croton punctatus, S. portulacastrum y S. edmondstonii, H. ritteriana, E. prostrata y Melochia crenata). Las especies calcifilas presentaron una fraccin de Ca soluble en agua 50% (S. martima, C mesembrianthemifolia, S. plumieri, H. curassavicum, Sporobolus virginicus y B. martima). El C revel cinco especies con metabolismo fotosinttico C4 (A. halimifolia, G. albiflora, S. virginicus, C. mesembrianthemifolia y A. oestophora). Los altos valores de N sugieren como fuente principal de N al NO del suelo. Este trabajo incluye una compilacin de especies de plantas superiores de la costa caribea de Venezuela con indicaciones sobre su carcter haloftico. To determine their degree of halophytism it was analyzed the mineral composition and stable isotopes (C, and N) of leaf material and associated soils of 18 species of coastal plant species in three locations in Falcon State, Venezuela (Coro-La Vela road, COVE; east coast of Paraguan, COP, and Tacuato bay in Paraguan, TAC). COP soils were sandy and had the lowest concentrations of N, P, K and Na. TAC soils showed higher salinity (Na, Mg and Ca), whereas those of COVE had higher N and P concentrations and clay texture. COP species had the highest Na concentrations and were more succulent (Sesuvium portulacastrum, S. edmondstonii, Bats martima, Sarcocornia perennis andHeterostachys ritteriana). Chamaesyce mesembrianthemifolia and Crotn punctatus had leaf K/Na ratios > 1 (non halophytes). Chamaesyce mesembrianthemifolia, Scaevola plumieri, Argusia gnaphalodes, Egletes prostrata, Suriana martima, and Gomphrena albiflora were relative K accumulators. Calciophobes accumulated most Ca in form of water insoluble oxalate (Atriplex oestophora, G. albiflora and Alternanthera halimifolia), or sequestered in form of phosphates and pectates (Croton punctatus, S. portulacastrum and S. edmondstonii, H. ritteriana, E. prostrata, and Melochia crenata). Calciophile species had a water soluble Ca fraction  50% (S. martima, C. mesembrianthemifolia, S. plumieri, H. curassavicum, Sporobolus virginicus and B. maritima). The C values revealed five species with C4-photosynthesis (A. halimifolia, G. albiflora, S. virginicus, C. mesembrianthemifolia ana A. oestophora). The positive values of N suggest soil NO as the main N source. This paper includes a compilation of higher plant species of the Caribbean coast of Venezuela with indications of their halophytic character.

El xilema axial y periaxial se distinguen por las siguientes caractersticas: El xilema axial tiene los vasos de menor dimetro y no est estratificado; el xilema periaxial, al contrario, tiene los vasos de mayor dimetro y est estratificado por capas parenquimticas ms delgadas alternantes con capas ms anchas de fibras. 8. Las capas concntricas de parnquima entrecaladas en el xilema periaxial tienen la funcin de aumentar la flexibilidad del leo. 9. Los vasos de dimetro ancho representan una caracterstica especial de los bejucos facilitando la conduccin de agua por mayores distancias. Alcanzan su mayor dimetro en el bejuco de cadena con 765 . 10. El floema que est estratificado en lber duro y lber blando en las formas arbreas de crecimiento normal en los bejucos consiste slo en lber blando o cuando se forma lber duro, ste est habitualmente disperso irregularmente dentro del lber blando. Sin embago, el floema no juega ningn papel en la estructura anmala y se queda siempre como una capa muy delgada. 11 . Por lo general, los ortsticos alternan con las salientes o protuberancias formadas en el eje y se las hallan, por lo tanto, en las depresiones o, si se las encuentran sobre las salientes, siempre se disponen en las salientes de menor tamao y donde hay los vasos de menor dimetro. Esto significa que las hojas estn o sobre el xilema axial o sobre el xilema periaxial de menor extensin y con los vasos menos anchos. 12. Sin embargo, en el bejuco de cadena se presenta tambin estratificacin del xilema periaxial. Los tallos adoptan forma ondulada por un favorecimiento alternativo del crecimiento hipo-o epitnico de manera que una vez el lado superior de la rama est favorecido desarrollndose las dos "alas" hacia arriba, mientras que en el prximo nudo se favorece el lado opuesto. La ondulacin viene claramente influida por la disposicin de las hojas, como lo demuestran las figs. 35-38. La flexibilidad de la rama en sentido transversal es casi nula, mientras que es grande en el plano mediano o sea a lo largo de la rfema, puesto que las ramas son aplanadas. El vrtice de una ondulacin se encuentra siempre sobre un nudo y, puesto que las hojas se encuentran una vez en el lado superior y en el nudo siguinte en el lado inferior, el eje forma ondulaciones alternantes hacia arriba y hacia abajo. La hoja tiene, por lo tanto, una influencia negativa sobre el desarrollo del xilema periaxial, ya que ste se desarrolla ms en el lado opuesto a la insercin de la hoja. 13. El xilema periaxial que sigue al xilema axial muestra un grado ms alto de diferenciacin. Cuando se forma muy tempranamente, como es el caso en el bejuco de cadena, de manera que el xilema axial queda sumamente reducido y casi todo el eje se compone de xitema periaxial, este qa rae ter es entonces una seal de que se trata de una estructura ms avanzada y ms especializada detede el punto de vista evolutivo, ya que est ms adaptada a la vida de bejuco. Cuando, al otro lado, el xilema periaxial se forma muy tarde durante el desarrollo del eje, esto significa que el tipo de bejuco se encuentra en una escala ms baja, desde el punto de vista de adaptacin, o sea que es ms primitivo y menos especializado. Bauhinia splendens var. latifolia representa, por lo tanto, una forma ms primitiva como liana y ms recientemente formada, desde el punto de vista filogentico, y ms parecida a las formas arbreas, puesto que el xilema periaxial se origina muy tarde en el eje. Puede decirse entonces que el xilema axial representa la forma de "juventud" del leo, mientras que el xilema periaxial representa la forma avanzada, ms diferenciada, ms especializada y adaptada a la vida del bejuco. 14. En resumen puede decirse que la estructura anmala en forma de costi I tas, salientes, protuberancias o alas viene influida en alto grado por la disposicin de las hojas. Es decir que la presencia d la hoja impide el desarrollo del xilema periaxial en alto grado cual ultimo se origina en los lugares ms lejos de las inserciones de las hojas. Este resultado coincide con observaciones anteriores de nosotras, p. e. en las Sapinadeae (Serjania) y en las Bignoniaceae (Macfadyena) donde la divisin del cuerpo leoso est dirigida por la disposicin de las hojas. 1. The axes of the studied arboreous forms of Bauhinia show radial symmetry, a normal growth in thickness, and stratified phloem with alternating layers of hard and soft tissue. The wood is of the porous diffuse type with vessels of an average diameter of 87  approximately. In the lateral branches, a distichous phyllotaxis is realized. 2. In the axes of the studied lianas belonging to the genus Bauhinia we observed at first a continuous vascular cylinder of regular structure which corresponds to the woody body of the above mentioned arboreous forms (fig. 4). 3. In the studied lianas of the genus Bauhinia, two different types of anomalous structure occur: a) One in which new layeds of cambium are formed successively from the periclyael, restriceted in their origin to certain parts of the axis where the protuberances develop. In the priphery of the protuberances of first order, a third cambium can be developed from the pericycel of the protuberance of first order to give rise to a protuberance of second order, so that the two protuberances are superposed one above the other. Up to three protuberances arranged in the form of stories could be observed (fig. 5). b) In the second type of anomalous secondary growth, it is the first and only vascular cambium which produces the protuberances, ribs or wings, since it is activated more vigorously in certain parts of the axis where the outgrowth forms. 4. In most of the studied lianas, the axis has bilateral or dorsiventral symmetry and is often flattened in the transverse plane. 5. The leaves are arranged in distichous manner in all studied examples and the orthostichies are obviously related to the anomalous structure, which means that the anomaly is affected by the position of the leaves. 6. In the second type of anomalous secondary growth, two different types of secondary xylem can be distinguished, that is to say: an axial xylem which forms first when the axis still shows normal shape; and a periaxial xylem surrounding the first one which produces the anomalous strurture. By the restricted activity of the cambium it forms either only in those parts where the growth is more vigorous or it forms at least in larger amounts where the ribs emerge. 7. The axial and the periaxial xylem are distinguished by the following characteristics: The axial xylem has vessels of a lesser diameter and is not stratified; the periaxial xylem, on the other hand, has the vessels of a larger diameter and is stratified by the occurrence of small parenchymatous layers which alternate with thicker layers of fibers. 8. The concentric layers of parenchyma inserted between the fiber layers of the periaxial xylem have the function to increase the flexibility of the wood. 9. The large vasseles of the periaxial xylem represent a special character of the lianas and facilitate the conduction of water over larger distances. They reach their largest diameter in the "chain liana" (or "staircase of monkeys"), "bejuco de cadena", with 765 . 10. The phloem consisting of soft and hard bast in the arboreous forms, is composed only of soft tissue in the climbing forms or, when hard bast is developed at all, this is present in losser quantities and is dispersed in a more irregular way. In all cases, the phloem is of no importance what-so-ever for the anomalous structure of the liana and is always restricted to a very small layer. 11. The orthoistiahies alternate with the ribs or protuberance of the axis and are consequently found in the depressions  or, in case the leaves form over the protuberances (Bauhinia guianensis, fig. 46), they apper over the smaller ones where the vessels are of a lesser diameter. This means that the leaves form where the axial xylem is or the periaxial xylem of lesser extension and smaller vessels develop. 12. In the "chain liana", the periaxial xylem is also stratified. The twigs adopt an undulate form by alternately favoured epi-or hypottonic growth so that one time the upper side of the twig is favoured, while in the following node the opposite side is favoured in its growth. The undulation is obviously affected by the position of the leaves, as the figs. 35-38 show. The flexibility of the axis in transversal direction is very low, while it is strong in the median plane, this is in longitudinal direction of the twig, as the twigs are flattened transversely. The crest of a wave coincides always with a node, and, as the leaves alternate on the upper and lower side of the branch, the axis bencomes undulated alternately toward the upper or lawer side. The leaves exercise consequently a negative influence over the developement of the periaxial xylem, since this develops better on the opposite side of the leaf insertion. 13. The periaxial xylem which follows the axial xylem in its development, shows a higer degree of differentiation. When it forms very early during development, as it is the case in the "chain liana" so that the axial xylem remains extremely reduced and almost the entire axis consists of periaxial xylem, this characteristic is a proof for the more advanced and more specialized type of liana, as seen from the evolutionary point of view, since it shows a better adaptation to the life form of lianas. When, on the other hand, the periaxial xylem forms very late during development of the axis, this prooves that the liana is of a lower degree, from the phylogenetic point of view, that it is more primitive and Jess specialized. Bauhinia splenderli var. latifolis, for example, represents a primitive form of liana, more recently developed from the phylogenetic point of view and more similar to the arboreous forms, as the periaxial xylem develops very late in this variety. One can therefore state that the axial xylem represents the "juvenile" form of the secondary xylem, while the periaxial xylem is the more advanced form, more differentiated, more specialized, and better adapted to the life form of lianas. 14. In summary we can say that the anomalous structure in Bauhinia in form of ribs, protuberances or wings is highly affected by the phyllotaxis. The presence of a leaf impedes apparently the development of the periaxial xylem to a high degree wich latter forms in the more remote spots from the leaf insertion. This result coincides with earlier observations of ours (Roth 1966, Roth in press) in the family, of Sapindaceae (Serjania) and in Bignoniaceae (Macfadyene) where the division of the woody body is affected by the position of the leaves.

Los caracteres comunes encontrados para la familia son: laticferos o clulas secretoras, abundancia de clulas ptreas en el lber duro, radios finos, sber con paredes en forma de "U" y drusas o cristales solitarios romboides. Dado el origen polifiltico de la familia Euphorbiaceae, los caracteres comunes encontrados pueden ser atribuidos al hbito arbreo de las especies estudiadas. This study analyzes the anatomical structure of the barks of 16 species of forestal trees of the Euphorbiaceace family from the rain forest of the Venezuelan Guayana. The shared characters found were: laticiferous or secretory cells, profusion of stone cells in hard bast, thin rays, suber with "U" shaped wall thickenings and druses or solitary rhomboidal crystals. Due to the polyphyletic origin of the Euphorbiaceae family, the shared characters found may be attributed to the arboreal habit of the studied species.

Esto indica que la reproduccin sexual es un evento que debe ocurrir en la poblacin estudiada, sin embargo el desbalance observado entre fases tetraspricas y gametofticas sugiere que mecanismos adicionales a la reproduccin sexual pudieran estar interactuando en el mantenimiento de la poblacin, uno de estos podra ser la baja viabilidad reportada para las tetrsporas de esta especie. Information on the reproductive phenology of Gelidium serrulatum J. Agardh, a red algal species with economical importance is given. In the studied population, during the whole year, the different phases of the life cycle of this species are presented: tetrasporophytes, male and female gametophytes, being tetrasporophytes more abundant than gametophytes, which implies an unbalance in the proportion 1:1 between them; on the other hand, the proportions among male and female gametophytes are similar. This indicates that the sexual reproduction is a probable event in the studied population; however, the unbalance observed between tetraspoprophytes and gametophytes suggest that additional mechanisms of reproduction could be interacting in the studied population's maintenance, one of these may be the reported low viability for tetraspores in this species.

41740987|Las Iridceas son una familia de plantas interesantes desde el punto de vista de la biologa reproductiva debido a que la diversidad de estructuras florales de sus especies atrae una variedad de visitantes florales. Para A. lahue y las especies de Sisyrinchium analizadas las estimaciones del sistema de apareamiento tienden a subestimar el grado de autogamia encontrado en experimentos previos. Iridaceae is an interesting plant family from the viewpoint of reproductive biology because the diverse floral structures of its species attract a gamut of different flower visitors. This work reports some reproductive aspects of five species of Iridaceae of the Salado river basin in the Argentine pampas: Cypella herbertii, Alophia lahue and three species of Sisyrinchium. C. herbertii exhibits a specialized interaction with oil-collecting bees, while the rest of the species studied had rather unspecialized visitors. For A. lahue and the species of Sisyrinchium analyzed estimations of expected mating system tend to underestimate the degree of autogamy found in previous experiments. Sin embargo, el crecimiento de la hoja es lento.

41740858|Se estudi la anatoma foliar en 15 especies de plantas vasculares que crecen en la zona costera del estado Falcn (Venezuela), a fin de analizar las caractersticas con potencial valor adaptativo en suelos salinos. El material foliar colectado se fij en FAA y posteriormente se efectuaron secciones transversales y macerados de la lmina. En la mayora de las especies estudiadas el desarrollo de tejido acufero en la epidermis y/o en el mesofilo es la principal caracterstica asociada con el habitat salino. Otros rasgos anatmicos de posible valor adaptativo son: presencia de tricomas, estomas protegidos por papilas, cristales en las clulas del mesofilo, estructuras secretoras y anatoma Kranz. The leaf anatomy of 15 species of vascular plants occurring in coastal zones of the Falcon State (Venezuela) was studied to evaluate the potential adaptive value of leaf anatomical features to the saline environment. Transverse sections and macerates of leaf material preserved in FAA were prepared for microscopic analysis. Results show that the development of water storing tissue in the mesophyll and/or epidermal cells is the main characteristic associated with the saline habitat in these species. Other characteristics of potential adaptive value are: presence of trichomes, stomata protected by papillae, crystals in mesophyll cells, secretory tissues, and Kranz anatomy.

41740992|En tres rboles de una poblacin natural de Acacia glomerosa se estudiaron las siguientes variables de la reproduccin sexual: nmero de flores por inflorescencia, de estambres por flor, de poliades por estambre, de polen por poliade, de pistilos con poliades viables y no viables, y nmero de tubos polinicos por poliade viable (TPP). Tambin se analiz el nmero de frutos por inflorescencia, de semillas por fruto y de vulos por ovario. Se encontr que el cociente polen/vulo fue 3699,14, el de semillas/vulo de 0,81 (seed-set) y el de frutos/flores por glomerulo 0,08 (fruit-set). Estos dos Ultimos cocientes indican que del total de vulos que produce una planta slo 6,5% (seed-set  fruit-set  100) pasan a semillas en polinizacin natural. Tanto el cociente polen/vulo elevado, como el porcentaje de vulos que pasan a semillas bajo, son congruentes con los resultados de la may oria de las especies algamas. El estudio de los estigmas en polinizacin natural revela que 35% no fueron polinizados, y de los que fueron polinizados cerca de 39% contenian poliades no viables. Estos resultados pueden indicar que los polinizadores en la poblacin son escasos, por no haberse encontrando diferencias significativas entre los tres rboles estudiados. Una moderada esterilidad de las poliades y/o de los pistilos podria estar limitando la fructifcacin. Los resultados de este estudio muestran que cuando los estigmas reciben una poliade viable un alto porcentaje de granos de polen fecundan los vulos del ovario. Esto hace que el numero de semillas que contienen los frutos desarrollados sea elevado (ca. 80% de los vulos del ovario pasan a semilla). Three trees of a natural population of Acacia glomerosa were studied. The following sexual reproduction variables were measured: number of flowers by inflorescence, number of stamens per flower, number of polyads per stamen, number of pollen per polyad, number of gynoecia with viable and no viable polyads, and numbers of pollen tubes per viable polyad growing at the styles (TPP). The number of fruits per inflorescence, number of seeds per fruit and number of ovules per ovary were also measured. It was found that the pollen/ovule ratio was 3699.14, the seeds/ovule ratio was 0.81 (seed-set), and the fruits/flower ratio per head was 0.08 (fruit-set). These two last ratios show that the total of ovules that produces a plant, only 6.5% (seed-set  fruit-set  100) becomes seeds in natural pollination. Not only the high pollen/ovule ratio, but also the low percentage of ovules that becomes seeds, are coherent with the results of the most of the allogarne species. The study of the stigmas in natural pollination reveals that 35% were not pollinated, and from those which were pollinated about 39% contained no viable polyads. These results might indicate that the pollinators in the population are limited, without finding important differences among the three trees studied. The moderate sterility of the polyads or the gynoecias, are both factors limiting the fruit-set. When the stigmas receive a viable polyad, a high percentage of pollen grain fertilizes the ovules of the ovary. This increases the number of seeds in the ripe fruits (ca. 80% of the ovules of ovary becomes a seed).

41740537|Se presenta una clave de campo para la identificacin de leguminosas leosas. Varios de los caracteres empleados tienen que ser observados en la planta entera por lo menos, en una de sus ramas; por eso la clave es mas bien "de campo" y no debe limitarse a fragmentos de plantas provenientes de un herbario. Los caracteres taxonmicos son definidos e ilustrados con lo necesario y lo suficiente para el ambito propuesto: la identificacin de las tribus. Se presentan tambin sugerencias sobre la sistematica de la familia. The author presents a field key for the identification of woody legumes. Several of the taxonomical characters employed have to be observed in the entire plant or at least in some of its branches. This "field key" will give poor results if used with portions of plants coming from herbaria. The taxonomical characters are defined and illustrated using the strict minimum for the identification of the tribes. Nevertheless it still remains impossible to make the distinction between some tribes of the Papilionoideae using vegetative and morphological characters alone. Finally, some suggestions and opinions are given about the systematic of the family.

We identified the visitors at the flowers of 25 forest species. The great majority of the species studied are day-flowering. The most common flower type was pleomorphic (35%), followed by stereomorphic (20%) and pseudo blossoms (20%), zygomorphic (19%) and stereomorphic combined with zygomorphic (6%). Bee pollination was the most common pollination syndrome (87.7%), butterfly pollination was a secondary syndrome in some bee-pollinated flowers and a primary syndrome in 15% of the flowers. Bird and wind pollination each accounted for 5.3% of the species. Three species of humming bird and 46 insect species were captured visiting flowers. Pollen was generally found ventrally on the bees, wasp and flies. The small bees visited the largest number of flower species. The majority of the plant species studied were generalist, although there were exceptions. The flies appeared to be move specific en their visits from the bees.

Con estas caractersticas se pueden identificar algunas especies de ambos gneros. El examen del tallo, tanto primario como secundario, no revel diferencias sustanciales entre las especies analizadas. Se aporta informacin original de las caractersticas de este rgano. El anlisis de los rganos reproductivos incluy la anatoma de todas las piezas florales. El fruto puede tener superficie lisa, verrucosa o tuberculada, lo cual depende de la estructura del pericarpio. Se observaron cinco tipos de pericarpio, dos tipos corresponden a frutos lisos, y los restantes a frutos verrucosos o tuberculados. The anatomical study of some species of the Venezuelan genera of Turneraceae Piriqueta and Turnera, is presented. The paper includes the analysis of indumentum, colleters, extrafloral nectaries, and the structure of primary stem, wood, leaf, flower and fruit. Material conserved in FAA was used, some species were worked with herborized material. The analysis was made on the basis of optical and scanning electronic microscopy. Glandular trichomes types microcapitate, capitate sessile and setiform were found. The non-glandular trichomes are simple, either unicellular or pluricellular uniseriate and porrect-stellate. The colleters present are standard and sessile types. The extrafloral nectaries can be elevated or flattened. The excretion of the nectar is transcuticular or through "pores". The anatomical characters of the leaves were: epidermal cells, position and type of the stomata, stomatal index, epidermal idioblasts, type of mesophyll, veins and type of bundle sheaths. With these characteristics some species of both genera can be identified. The analysis of the primary and secondary stem does not reveal substantial differences among the analysed species. Original information of the characteristics of this organ is provided. The analysis of the reproductive organs included the anatomy of all the floral pieces. The presence and combination of these characters, in addition to other features like fruit anatomy, allow the characterisation of different taxa in both genera. The fruit surface can be flat, warty or tuberculated, which depends on the structure of the pericarp. Seven pericarp types were observed, two types correspond to flat fruits, and the rest to warty or tuberculated fruits. The results show that certain characters like indment, foliar and fruit anatomy are of greater utility to differentiate the species from the studied genera.

41740722|Se presentan observaciones citogenticas en plantas mantenidas como germoplasma in vitro, callo, embriones somticos y plntulas regeneradas de stos durante el proceso de embriognesis somtica indirecta de papa (Solanum tuberosum L. cv. Dsire) en medio solidificado con gelrite. Las plantas madres utilizadas como donantes para los explantes, presentan en sus races el nmero euploide de cromosomas de este cultivar (2n= 4x= 48), sin embargo, en el callo se observan abundantes clulas binucleadas, con la consecuente mixoploida en los tejidos y clulas que se acercan al nmero octoploide de cromosomas. Se propone que en este caso la poliploidizacin de ciertas clulas ocurre por cariocinesis no acompaada de citocinesis, formndose clulas binucleadas, seguida de divisiones celulares simultneas en los dos ncleos (bimitosis), producindose en algunos casos por desorganizacin parcial de los husos acromticos metafases multipolares con cromosomas dispersos. Entre la poblacin de plntulas regeneradas de los callos algunas presentan desarrollo anmalo y su examen citogentico revela de nuevo mixoploidia en sus tejidos. Cytogenetic observations are presented in plants maintained as in vitro germplasm, callus, somatic embryos and regenerated plantlets during the process of indirect somatic embryogenesis of potato (Solanum tuberosum L. cv. Dsire) in culture medium solidified with gelrite. The mother plants used as donors for the expiants present in their roots the euploid number of chromosomes of this cultivar (2n= 4x= 48), however in callus abundant binucleated cells are observed, with the consequent mixoploidy in the tissues and cells that come closer to the octoploid number of chromosomes. In this case the polyploidization of certain cells takes place due to caryokinesis not accompanied by cytokinesis, being formed binucleated cells, followed by simultaneous cellular divisions in the two nuclei (bimitosis). In some cases -for partial disorganization of the achromatic spindlesmultipolar metaphases with dispersed chromosomes are produced. Among the population of regenerated plantlets of the callus, several ones present anomalous development and their cytogenetic examination reveals again mixoploidy in their tissues.

Bosques altos con dominancia de Clathrotropis glaucophylla, Protum trifoliolatum y Osteophloeum platyspermum, 3. Bosques sobre afloramientos granticos con dominancia de Virola sebifera, Eschweilera subglandulosa, Protium macrospermum y Qualea paraensis. Se incluye un listado por familias de las especies registradas en el rea y se presentan comentarios florsticos, fitogeogrficos y de diversidad de las especies en relacin con la flora de reas adyacentes a la Guayana y Amazonia venezolana. Finalmente, se demuestra el valor de los trabajos de campo del proyecto inventario de la regin Guayana (PIRNRG) para la botnica tropical, en virtud que antes de comenzar con esta actividad muchas especies de rboles y lianas citadas en el presente trabajo eran desconocidas para el rea de La Esmeralda, la Amazonia y Guayana venezolana. The present study was conducted within the scope of a field work program of a natural resource survey project carried out by CVG-TECMIN, C.A. in the Amazonian region and the Venezuelan Guayana Shield. Based on three 0.5-hectare forestry surveys, general botanical collections, and "in situ" observations, the floristic composition of three different nonflooded forest types is described. These forests are situated over hills aproximately 15 km NE of La Esmeralda, (03 08' Lat. N; 65 27' Long. W), upper Orinoco, Amazonas State, Venezuela, and were classified as: 1. Evergreen forest dominated by Mouriri collocarpa, Oenocarpus bataua, and Virola elongata, 2. Evergreen forest dominated by Clathrotropis glaucophylla, Protium trifoliolatum, and Osteophloeum platyspermum, 3. Evergreen forest on hills upon granite outcrops dominated by Virola sebifera, Eschweilera subglandulosa, Protium macrospermum and Qualea paraensis. A list of the species collected in the area as well as comments on the phytogeographical relationships of the reported species relating to adjacent floras are also given. Many tree and liana canopy species were previously unknown to both the Esmeralda area and the Venezuelan Amazonia. This demonstrates clearly the contribution of CVG-TECMIN's field work to neotropical botany.

41740812|Se realiz un anlisis dendrocronolgico de tres especies de Tachigali y dos de Terminalia para estimar su crecimiento radial. En el bosque siempreverde, el crecimiento fue 5,48  2,74 mm/ao para Tachigali sp. 1 y 3,23  0,63 mm/ao para Terminalia cf. amazonia, con tasas de densidad de madera menores para la primera (0,432  0,04 g/cm) y mayores para la segunda (0,708  0,05 g/cm). En el bosque semideciduo Tachigali cf. guianensis present 5,85  0,49 mm/ao y 0,683  0,07 g/cm y Terminalia amazonia 2,40  0,24 mm/ao y 0,705  0,03 g/cm. A pesar de algunas limitaciones, los resultados indican la aplicabilidad del mtodo en bosques con poca estacionalidad, cuando los anillos presentan un nivel aceptable de nitidez. A dendrochronological analysis was carried out for three species of Tachigali and two of Terminalia to estimate radial growth. In the evergreen forest, Tachigali sp. 1 grew 5,48  2,74 mm/year and Terminalia cf. amazonia 3,23  0,63 mm/year. The wood density rate of the first species was low (0,432  0,04 g/cm), and the second high (0,708  0,05 g/cm). In the semideciduous forest, Tachigali cf. guianensis grew 5,85  0,49 mm/year and Terminalia amazonia 2,40  0,24 mm/year, the wood density was 0,683  0,07 g/cm and 0,705  0,03 g/cm, respectively. Dendrochronology represents, with some limitations, a viable approach appliable in forests with no seasonality, when growth rings show enough sharpness.

43957303|Se realiz un estudio etnobotnico en una comunidad indgena Piapoco en el norte de la Amazonia colombiana, con el objetivo de documentar los usos y manejo de las palmas. Atravs de inventarios, caminatas etnobotnicas y talleres se registraron 28 especies, 23 de ellas asociadas con algn uso. Del total de 44 usos hallados, se destacaron la elaboracin de techos, paredes, consumo de frutos, bebidas, la cria de larvas de colepteros, y morrales de transporte. Las palmas silvestres consideradas ms importantes por los Piapoco de acuerdo al ndice de Importancia Relativa (IR) faeron Attalea butyracea, A. maripa, Euterpeprecatoria, Oenocarpus bacaba, O. bataua y Socratea exorrhiza, las cuales se encuentran bajo presin debido a que su cosecha es principalmente destructiva. An ethnobotanical study of the palms used by the Piapoco indigenous people inhabiting the northern fringe of the Amazon forest in Colombia was carried out. Through inventories, ethnobotanical walks, and workshops, 28 palm species were recorded, 23 of which were used. For these species 44 uses were recorded; the most important were thatching, wall construction, fruit consumption, beverage preparation, breeding of edible beetle larvae, and manufacture of carrying bags. The palms considered most important according to their Relative Importance Index (RI) were Attalea butyracea, A. maripa, Euterpe precatoria, Oenocarpus bacaba, O. bataua, and Socratea exorrhiza, which are under strong pressure because their harvest is mostly destructive.

41740989|Debido al escaso conocimiento sobre la biologa reproductiva del gnero Chamaecrista (Caesalpinioideae - Leguminosae), se estudiaron las especies herbceas Ch. serpens y Ch. nictitans subsp. patellaria var.paraguariensis a fin de generar informatin de base sobre sus sistemas reproductivo y de apareamiento, considerando la relacin polen/vulo, la asignacin de biomasa floral, la eficiencia natural en la produccin de frutos y semillas y la eficacia reproductiva. Los resultados indican que ambas especies son parcialmente autocompatibles y parcialmente autgamas. Sin embargo, la alta relacin polen/vulo y la asignacin de biomasa principalmente a la funcin de atraccin y a la funcin masculina en ambas especies reflejan la necesidad de la visita de polinizadores, los cuales parecen ser altamente efectivos en las poblaciones estudiadas dada la alta eficiencia naturai en la produccin de frutos y semillas y la alta eficacia reproductiva mostrada por ambas especies. Due to the scant knowledge about the reproductive biology of the genus Chamaecrista (Caesalpinioideae - Leguminosae), the two herbaceous species Ch. serpens and Ch. nictitans subsp. patellaria var. paraguariensis were studied in order to produce basic information about their breeding and mating systems, considering the pollen/ovule ratio, floral biomass allocation to floral functions, natural efficiency in fruit and seed production and reproductive efficacy. The results show that both species are partially self-compatible and partially autogamous. Nevertheless, the high polen/ovule ratio and the biomass allocation mainly to attraction and male functions showed the necessity of the visit of pollinators, which seem to be quite effective in the studied populations due to the high natural efficiency in fruit and seed production and the high reproductive efficacy showed by both species.

La formacin de cristales con tanta regularidad y en determinada posicin que se presenta como carcter constante es sumamente rara en la corteza.

41740986|El objetivo de esta investigatin embriolgica, la primera realizada en el gnero, fue tipificar el proceso de microsporogenesis en Hymenocallis caribaea. La meiosis se desarrolla cuando los botones florales an se encuentran dentro del bulbo. La microsporogenesis sigue un patron de tipo sucesivo, comun en las monocotiledneas. El proceso es asincrnico entre yemas de una misma inflorescencia (indeterminado o acrpeto), anteras de una misma flor, y entre el apice y la base de la misma antera (basipeto). Las anteras poseen estomas, el tapete es de tipo ameboide periplasmodial y las clulas del endotecio no desarrollan engrosamientos en la pared, al contrario de lo que ocurre en la mayoria de los reprsentantes de la familia. El tapete invade tempranamente la cavidad de la antera y produce pollenkit, una secretion amarillenta de tipo lipidico que se deposita sobre los granos de polen maduros confirindoles propiedades adhrentes. Las micrsporas son uninucleadas, con patron de ornamentation incipiente al momento de ser liberadas de la ttrada. Los granos de polen son monocolpados, como en la mayor parte de las monocotiledneas; la exina tiene un patron de ornamentation denso en los extremos y un reticulo ms laxo en la zona centrai. Al momento de la dehiscencia de la antera el polen es binucleado, condicin que se considera ancestral en las angiospermas junto a la presencia de estomas en las anteras. An embryological investigation was undertaken for the first time in a member of the genus Hymenocallis, to describe the microsporogenesis in Hymenocallis caribaea. Meiosis takes place when flower buds are still inside the bulb. Microsporogenesis follows a successive type, common in monocots. The process is asynchronous between buds of the same inflorescence (undeterminate or acropetal), anthers of the same flower, and between the apex and the base of each anther (basipetal). Anthers have stornata, the tapetum is ameboid, or periplasmodial, and the endothecium doesn't develop wall thickenings, contrary to what happens in most family representatives. Tapetum invades anther cavity early and produces pollenkit, a yellowish lipid secretion which is deposited over the mature pollen grains giving them adherent properties. When released from tetrads, microspores are uninucleate and show an undeveloped pattern of wall sculpturing. Pollen grains are monosulcate as in most monocots; the exine shows a dense sculpturing pattern at the ends and a loose reticulum at the central zone. At the time of anther dehiscence, pollen is binucleate, a condition which is considered ancestral within the angiosperms as is the presence of stornata in the anthers.
41740603|El pericarpio del fruto se subdivide en el exocarpio o flavedo que contiene las cavidades de aceite, el mesocarpio esponjoso o albedo, y el endocarpio delgado del cual proceden las papilas jugosas. Los estomas de la epidermis externa del fruto son del tipo actinoctico. La mayor parte de la cscara es colenquimatosa. Las papilas empiezan a formarse en un fruto de un dimetro aproximado de 3 mm o menos en las paredes tangenciales internas de los lculos. Primero se observa un alargamiento anticlinal de ciertas clulas epidrmicas que ms tarde se dividen periclinalmente En la formacin de la parte basal pueden tambin participar clulas subepidrmicas. Toda la epidermis es meristemtica en esta etapa y se divide periclinalmente de manera que toda la zona subepidrmica puede considerarse como formacin epidrmica. El pednculo de las papilas crece en longitud por divisiones transversales de clulas que luego se alargan paralelamente a eje longitudinal del pednculo. El extremo es ms meristemtico y se compone de clulas ms pequeas y ms ricas en protoplasma; por divisiones periclinales a la superficie de las capas subepidrmica se ensancha el extremo o cabeza. A los lados de las papilas se desarrollan simultneamente con stas, pelos pluricelulares ramificados con clulas terminales grandes y con membranas engrosadas. Estos pelos son tambin formaciones epidrmicas, pero se distinguen en su desarrollo de las papilas, ya desde el principio. Por lo tanto, no pueden ser interpretados como primordios abortivos de las papilas. Adems, se encuentran pelos unicelulares (o filas de clulas) en los canales estilares. Ambos tipos de pelos segregan posiblemente muclago. La simetra del fruto es estrictamente radial y los procesos de crecimiento estn adaptados a esta simetra. En el fruto joven se forman hileras radiales de clulas por divisiones periclinales continuas de todas las clulas del fruto; no se puede ubicar ningn meristemo especial. Ms tarde, acta el crecimiento de dilatacin, especialmente en el albedo donde se alargan los brazos de las clulas considerablemente, y las hileras radiales desaparecen. Al principio, la cascara aumenta mucho en anchura, mientras que los lculos quedan pequeos. Luego pasa todo lo contrario; la cascara cesa en el crecimiento y los lculos se extienden en direccin radial. La cascara disminuye finalmente en anchura por la dilatacin del tejido esponjoso del albedo y la extensin radial de los lculos. Las clulas debajo de la epidermis externa quedan ms pequeas y ms meristemticas por ms tiempo y se adaptan al crecimiento de dilatacin por divisiones celulares en varios planos. Almidn no se encuentra ms en un fruto de un dimetro de 3 mm, pero cristales de heperidina en forma de abanico o forma dendroide se presentan en abundancia en todas las partes del fruto joven ; sin embargo, desaparecen en frutos de etapas ms avanzadas.

41740775|En abril de 1783 fue enviada a Amrica por el emperador Joseph II de Austria una expedicin liderada por el botnico austraco y profesor de Historia Natural Franz Joseph Mrter, con el objeto de aumentar las colecciones de los museos, zoolgicos y jardines botnicos de la corte. In April 1783 an expedition led by the Austrian botanist and professor of Natural History, Franz Joseph Marter, was sent to America by Emperor Joseph II of Austria. The purpose of this trip was to enlarge the collections of the museums, zoos and botanical gardens of the Imperial Court. Besides the leader, the expedition also counted on the presence of a doctor, a painter and the Imperial gardeners, Franz Bredemeyer and Franz Boos. At later stages of the journey, specifically during the stays in Haiti and Venezuela, there appeared another gardener, called Josef Schcht, who apparently formed no part of the original list of expedition members. Papers dealing with botanical collectors make reference to the presence of Bredemeyer and Schcht in Venezuela. However, Boos is not mentioned with regard to this country, even though there are reports of samples collected by him in this land. The existence of a document, dated 1787, held in the "Archivo General de la Nacin" (the National Archives), Caracas, Venezuela, in which both Boos and Schcht are mentioned, could signify proof of their presence in Venezuelan territory. In this present work a partial transcription of the abovementioned document is included. Besides this, pertinent historical observations are made about the collecting endeavors of the Austrian naturalists, as well as regarding the botanical names linked to their surnames.
41740991|Stenocereus griseus y Cereus repandus son dos de las cactceas columnares ms abundantes y ampliamente distribuidas en las regiones ridas y semiridas de Venezuela. A pesar de su valor como especies clave para la fauna silvestre y de su potencial valor econmico, la informacin sobre su actividad reproductiva y capacidad de regeneracin es muy limitada. Stenocereus griseus and Cereus repandus are two of the most abundant and widely distributed columnar cacti in the arid and semiarid regions of Venezuela. Despite their value as keystone species for wildlife and their potential economic value, information on their reproductive activity and regeneration capacities is quite limited. These aspects were evaluated in natural populations from Padre Diego, Lara State, and Paraguana Peninsula, Falcon State. These cacti have broad time windows for reproduction and considerably high fecundity levels (S. griseus: 44,225 seeds/ind, C. repandus: 322,749 seeds/ind), which confer them great advantages in terms of natural regeneration and propagation. These species depend on nurse plants for their establishment. The highest percentages of survival occurred under the shadow of trees. Under natural conditions, these species can produce half a ton of fruit pulp per hectare.

Sin embargo, todo el material analizado regenerado in vitro (embriones somticos y plntulas) present un nmero cromosmico estable (2n = 44) igual al de las plantas madres. The chromosome number variation is one of several factors that can play an important role in the production of somaclonal variants. To confirm the stability of chromosome number in coffee hybrid Catimor (Coffea arabica cv. Red Caturra  Hybrid of Timor) somatic embryos and plantlets were regenerated through indirect somatic embryogenesis from leaf expiants, chromosomes were counted in cell of somatic embryos, root apexes of in vitro regenerated plantlets and root apexes of zygotic embryos from mother plants (Hybrid Catimor). The same procedure was performed on cultivars related to the coffee hybrid Catimor. Fixation was done in Carnoy and staining by the carbolfuchsin method. The following chromosome numbers were confirmed: Coffea canephora cv. Robusta: 2n = 22; Hybrid of Timor (C. arabica  canephora): 2n = 44; arabica cv. Red Caturra: 2n = 44 and Hybrid Catimor: 2n = 44. In somatic embryos and in vitro plantlets, chromosomes in mitotic metaphase were in appearance more densely grouped and thicker than in mother plants. Nevertheless, the chromosome number in all the samples from tissues regenerated in vitro (somatic embryos and plantlets) had stable chromosome number (2n = 44).

Coconut (Cocos nucifera) is a monoic species with a large one-seeded fruit that is commercialized in all tropical regions. A study of the anatomic structure of staminate and pistillate flowers was carried out in order to complement the knowledge on the reproductive biology of this species. 41740756|Este trabajo presenta el estudio anatmico xilemtico de 17 especies de la familia Anacardiaceae: Anacardium excelsum, A. spruceanum, Astronium graveolens, A. obliquum, A. ulei, Campnosperma gumifera, Cyrtocarpa velutinifolia, Loxopterygium sagotii, Mangifera indica, Mauria heterophylla, Ochoterenaea colombiana, Spondias lutea, S. mombin, Rhus striata, Tapirira guianensis, T. obtusa y Thyrsodium spruceanum. This paper deals about wood anatomy of seventeen species from Anacardiaceae family in Venezuela: Anacardium excelsum, A. spruceanum, Astronium graveolens, A. obliquum, A. ulei, Campnosperma gumifera, Cyrtocarpa velutinifolia, Loxopterygium sagotii, Mangifera indica, Mauria heterophylla, Ochoterenaea colombiana, Spondias lutea, S. mombin, Rhus striata, Tapirira guianensis, T. obtusa and Thyrsodium spruceanum. From here on the quality of the grass droped dawn drastically; an aceptable nutritive value was found until the end of the sixth month; in the remaining six months the "paja peluda" showed very poor nutritive value. 41740820|Stylosanthes capitata (Leguminosae) es una especie de importancia en la vegetacin de sabanas de Venezuela. Esta especie perenne, que extiende su rango de distribucin hacia el subtrpico de Amrica del Sur (10 N-22 S), se ha reportado solamente en Brasil y Venezuela. Es resistente a la sequa, pudiendo aumentar el perodo de crecimiento hasta nueve meses en climas con sequas bien definidas. Debido a la importancia econmica y ecolgica de esta leguminosa forrajera, a su presencia de acuerdo a patrones estacionales, y a la relevancia de la propagacin in vitro como herramienta de utilidad en la conservacin de recursos filogenticos, es importante desarrollar un proceso de propagacin in vitro ptimo para la especie que permita su disponibilidad todo el ao. Para el ensayo se utilizaron como explante yemas florales, y como medio base, sales de Murashige & Skoog (1962), enriquecido con vitaminas como tiamina (5 mg/1), mioinositol (100 mg/1) y cido nicotnico (1mg/1). Adicionalmente se aadi sacarosa (30 g/1) como fuente de carbohidratos y agar (8 g/1) como sustancia gelificante. Se emplearon dos concentraciones de BA (Bencilaminopurina) como fuente de citocinina (0,25 y 0,50 mg/1) para la fase de iniciacin, observndose en la concentracin de 0,50 mg/1 los primeros cambios morfogneticos a los 60 das de la siembra de los explantes. En la fase de multiplicacin se utilizaron dos concentraciones de citocinina, 0,50 mg/1 y 1 mg/1. Esta ltima concentracin paraliza la evolucin de los explantes y reduce el nmero de brotes por explante. En la etapa de enraizamiento, al utilizar 0,50 mg/1 de IBA (cido indolbutirco) y eliminar la citocinina se obtuvo un desarrollo adecuado del sistema radical. Las plntulas obtenidas fueron aclimatadas y trasladadas con xito a condiciones de vivero. Stylosanthes capitata (Leguminosae) is a species of great importance in the vegetation of savannas of Venezuela. This perennial species which extends its range of distribution toward the subtropical area of South America (10 N-22 S), has been reported only in Brazil and Venezuela. It is resistant to drought, being able to extend its growing period to nine months in climates where droughts are well defined. Due to the ecological and economic importance of this forage legume, and the use of in vitro propagation as a tool of utility for the conservation of phytogenetic resources and its presence according to seasonal periods, it is of importance to develop an optimum process of in vitro propagation for this species that allows its availability all year around. For testing purposes floral buds as explants, and Murashige & Skoog (1962) salts as base medium supplemented with vitamins as thiamine (5 mg/1), myoinositol (100 mg/1) and nicotinic acid (1 mg/1) were used. Additionally sucrose (30 g/1) as source of carbohydrates and agar (8 g/1) as gelling medium were added. Two concentrations of BA (Bencilaminopurine) were employed as source of cytokinin (0.25 and 0.50 mg/1) as the initiation phase. The first morphogenetic changes appeared after 60 days of the expiants initiation at the concentration of 0.50 mg/1. In the multiplication phase two concentrations of cytokinins were used (0.50 mg/1 and 1 mg/1), at higher concentration of this hormone (1 mg/1 of BA) the evolution of the explants is paralyzed and the number of buds by explant is reduced. In the rooting phase when 0.50 mg/1 of IBA (indolbutiric acid) were used and no cytokinin in the medium an adequate development of the radical system was obtained. The obtained seedlings were then acclimated and transferred with success to greenhouse conditions.

No existe relacin aparente entre el tipo de ornamentacin de la exina y el sindrome de polinizacin. Pollen morphology of 19 species of Cleome L. (Capparidaceae, Cleomoideae) from Venezuela was examined by scanning electron microscopy. The pollen grains are tricolporate and variable in exine sculpturing. Six pollen types were identified on the basis of the exine sculpturing: I. Microequinate or equinate on the whole surface; II. Psilate in the polar region and microequinate in the remaining exine; III. Psilate in the polar region and insulate-microequinate in the remaining exine; IV. Verrucate; V. Rugulate; VI. Microreticulate. The exine sculpturing has diagnostic value within the genus and supports the classification of species into sections. It was found that species with similar pollen sculpturing have different pollination mechanisms and species with different types of pollen sculpturing can exhibit similar mechanisms of pollination. Apparently, there is not relationship between exine sculpturing and pollination syndromes.

41740892|La floracin, produccin de frutos inmaduros y de frutos maduros fueron evaluadas para 171 especies pertenecientes a 57 familias de angiospermas presentes en la vegetacin de la Estacin Biolgica de los Llanos. El objetivo de este estudio me establecer la correlacin entre la fenologa reproductiva y seis variables climticas de acuerdo a la forma de vida, hbitat y a nivel comunitario. Los valores mensuales de precipitacin y humedad relativa estn positivamente correlacionados, y los valores mensuales de evaporacin y temperatura estn negativamente correlacionados con el nmero de lianas, hierbas perennes y hierbas anuales con flores, mientras que lo contrario fue encontrado para el nmero de rboles con flores. El nmero de especies con flores est negativamente correlacionado con la temperatura y la evaporacin, y positivamente correlacionado con la humedad relativa y la precipitacin para las areas de transicin bosque-sabana, sabana, rea perturbada y para la comunidad. Los valores de insolacin estn negativamente correlacionados con la floracin en el bosque y en la transicin bosque-sabana. Slo la precipitacin est positivamente correlacionada con el nmero de especies con flores en el bosque. El nmero de especies con frutos inmaduros tiene correlacin positiva con la humedad relativa para arbustos, hierbas perennes y hierbas anuales, y con la precipitacin para arbustos y hierbas perennes. Por el contrario, el nmero de especies con frutos inmaduros est negativamente correlacionado con la radiacin para rboles, temperatura para especies herbceas, y evaporacin para arbustos y especies herbceas. El nmero de lianas con frutos inmaduros slo est negativamente correlacionado con la temperatura. El nmero total de especies de plantas con frutos inmaduros est negativamente correlacionado con la temperatura y evaporacin en los cuatro hbitats, y positivamente con la humedad relativa a nivel comunitario. El nmero de especies con frutos inmaduros est negativamente correlacionado con la radiacin y positivamente con la precipitacin en el rea del bosque. El nmero de arbustos y hierbas perennes con frutos maduros tuvo correlacin negativa con la temperatura y la evaporacin, y positiva con la humedad relativa. El nmero de lianas con frutos maduros est negativamente correlacionado con la humedad relativa y la precipitacin, y positivamente correlacionado con la evaporacin. El nmero de especies con frutos maduros slo est positivamente correlacionado con la radiacin para el rea de bosque. La fenologia reproductiva est positivamente correlacionada con las variables climticas asociadas con la disponibilidad de agua y negativamente con las variables climticas asociadas con la defciencia de agua. Estas correlaciones sugieren que la fenologa reproductiva puede covariar con atributos particulares del clima dependiendo de la forma de vida y hbitat de la comunidad. Flowering, unripe fruit production, and fruit maturation were evaluated for 171 species belonging to 57 families of angiosperms in the vegetation of the Venezuelan Central Plains at Estacin Biologica de los Llanos. The main goal of this study was to establish the correlation between reproductive phenology and six climatic variables according to plant life form, habitat, and overall community. Monthly values of precipitation and relative humidity are positively correlated, and monthly values of evaporation and temperature are negatively correlated with the number of lianas, perennial herbs, and annual herbs, the contrary was found for the number of tree species with flower. The number of plant species with flowers was negatively correlated with temperature and evaporation, and positively correlated with relative humidity and precipitation for forest-savanna transition, savanna, disturbed area, and overall community. Insolation was negatively correlated with flowering in the forest and forest-savanna transition. Precipitation was only correlated with the number of flowering plant species in the forest. The number of species with unripe fruits was positively correlated with the relative humidity for shrubs, perennial herbs, and annual herbs, and with precipitation for shrubs and perennial herbs. On the contrary, species with unripe fruits was negatively correlated with radiation for trees, temperature for herbaceous species, and evaporation for shrubs and herbaceous species. The number of lianas with unripe fruits was only correlated with temperature. The total number of species with unripe fruits was negatively correlated with temperature and evaporation for the four habitats, and positively correlated with the relative humidity at the community level. In addition, unripe fruits were negatively correlated with radiation and positively correlated with precipitation in the forest. Fruit maturation of shrubs and perennial herbs were negatively correlated with temperature and evaporation, and positively correlated with relative humidity. In addition, fruit maturation of lianas were negatively correlated with relative humidity and precipitation and positively correlated with evaporation. The number of plant species with ripe fruits was only positively correlated with radiation for the forest. In general, the reproductive phenology was positively correlated with climatic variables related to water availability and negatively with the climatic variables associated with water deficiency. These correlations suggest that reproductive phenology may co-vary according to particular attributes of the climate depending upon plant life form and the habitat of the community.

41740691|The center of generic diversity of the monocot family Xyridaceae is northern South America, where four of the five genera are endemic. Many species of these four small genera have restricted distributions and have not been critically studied, including the monospecific genus Aratitiyopea. Populations of this unusual Xyridaceae occur in mid-elevation, forested montane sites. Most Xyridaceae occur in exposed habitats, and although they are at least seasonally wet, many species exhibit xeromorphic adaptations. In contrast, Aratitiyopea presents a morphology and internal anatomy of a mesophyte (trailing stems, leaves with a relatively broad lamina, little mechanical tissue, and lacking a hypodermis, the latter two features present in other Xyridaceae with bifacial leaves) as well as effects of seasonal drying (cell death in the root and thickened endodermal cell walls). Structural details of the vegetative body of Aratitiyopea are presented here, and compared to that known for other Xyridaceae. Although the "gestalt" of Aratitiyopea is aberrant in Xyridaceae, it is structurally consistent with the family, and unusual features are interpreted as adaptations to its habitat, which few other Xyridaceae occupy. El centro de mayor diversidad genrica de la familia Xyridaceae se encuentra al norte de Amrica del Sur, donde se han detectado cuatro gneros endmicos de los cinco reconocidos en la familia. Muchos taxones representativos de estos gneros endmicos tienen una distribucin geogrfica restringida y no se han estudiado crticamente, incluyendo la nica especie del gnero Aratitiyopea. Poblaciones de esta Xyridaceae extraordinaria se encuentran a elevaciones medias en bosques montaosos. La mayora de las Xyridaceae se encuentran en ambientes expuestos, oligotrficos y que a pesar de ser al menos estacionalmente hmedos, muchas especies muestran adaptaciones xeromrficas. En contraste, Aratitiyopea presenta caractersticas morfolgicas y de anatoma interna particulares de un mesfito (tallos rastreros, hojas con una lmina relativamente ancha, poco tejido mecnico y la falta de una hipodermis presente en otras Xyridaceae con hojas bifaciales) as como efectos de resecamiento estacional (muerte de clulas en la raz y engrosamiento de las paredes celulares endodermales). En este trabajo se presentan estudios morfolgicos y anatmicos de las partes vegetativas de Aratitiyopea y se comparan con estudios previos de otros miembros de las Xyridaceae. Aunque el aspecto general de Aratitiyopea es aberrante en Xyridaceae, el gnero es estructuralmente con sistente con la familia, y los caracteres poco usuales son interpretados como adaptaciones a su ambiente tpico que comparte con muy pocas otras Xyridaceae.

Macfadyena unguis-cati is a species of liana that produces pod-like fruits consisting of two carpels and bearing winged seeds. This study was motivated by the diversity of capsule types and the few seed studies conducted in Bignoniaceae. Flowers and fruits in different development stages were structurally analyzed, following standard plant anatomical techniques. The fruit is a capsule with septifragal dehiscence associated with a septicidal dehiscence. During pre-anthesis, a meristem is formed in the middle region of the ovary mesophyll. The seed originates from an anatropous, unitegmic, tenuinucellate and endothelial ovule. The mature seed is exotestal and presents little endosperm and a straight embryo.

Las flores abren progresivamente desde las 6:00 h hasta las 10:00 h con una longevidad de cuatro dias. El nmero promedio de flores abiertas por inflorescencia es de 3 (1-6). La secrecin de nctar se inicia entre las 14:30 y 15:00 h, el volumen mximo producido es de 1 l/h. Las flores son visitadas por abejas carpinteras (Xylocopa sp.), Apis melifera, y hormigas (Solenopsis sp.). La actividad de los visitantes fue diurna y Xylocopa sp. estableci contacio directo con el estigma. Ms del 50% de la biomasa floral es asignada a la corola y por tanto a la atraccin. La relacin biomasa reproductiva/biomasa vegetativa fue de 0,28 indicando un desbalance entre el perianto y las partes reproductivas. Los cruces controlados indican que C. micans es autgama, sin embargo, las caracteristicas de inversion de biomasa y la relacin Polen/vulo sugieren un sistema reproductivo xengamo. El comportamiento autgamo se explica como una conducta consecuente con la historia de vida de la planta y su supervivencia en ambientes perturbados. La comparacin de los rasgos reproductivos de C. micans en el rea estudiada no difiere de los expresados en un estudio similar realizado previamente en una zona templada suramericana, lo cual indica que la variacin geogrfica no representa un factor que condicione el comportamiento reproductivo de la especie. The reproductive biology of Crotalaria micans was studied in disturbed areas of the remainder of cloudy forest of Altos de Pipe (IVIC), Miranda State, Venezuela. The flowers open progressively from the 6:00 h until the 10:00 h with a longevity of four days. The average number of flowers opened by inflorescence were 3 (1-6). The secretion of nectar begins between the 14:30 and 15:00 h, the maximum volume is 1 l/h. The flowers are visited by carpenter bees (Xylocopa sp.), Apis melifera, and ants (Solenopsis sp.). The activity of the visitors occur during the morning and afternoon. Xylocopa sp. was the visitor that established direct contact with the stigma. More than 50% of floral biomass is allocated to the corolla, and therefore to attraction. Reproductive/vegetative biomass ratio was 0,28, which indicate an unbalanced biomass allocation between perianth and reproductive parts. However, the characteristics of investment of biomass and the Pollen/Ovule ratio do not coincide with the results of the controlled crossings and they suggest a xenogamous reproductive system. The autogamous behavior is explained as consequent with the history of life of the plant and its survival in perturbed atmospheres. The comparison of the reproductive trait of micans in the studied area does not differ of the features expressed in a similar study carried out previously in a temperate South American area; this indicates that the geographical variation does not represent a factor that influences the reproductive behavior of the species.
