41740889|Para caracterizar el comercio de plantas medicinales en Caracas, Venezuela, se visitaron cinco mercados populares y 10 herbolarios, entrevistando los vendedores para determinar las especies comercializadas, usos tradicionales, su versatilidad e importancia relativa. Se registraron 198 especimenes, identificndose 164 especies, de 72 familias. La mayora son cultivadas, pero tambin se comercializan especies silvestres provenientes de los Andes y Guayana. Se registraron 120 usos, distribuidos en 18 categorias de enfermedades, principalmente del sistema digestivo, infecciosas y parasitarias, piel y tejido subcutneo. Predominaron las especies multipropsito (164, IVF > 0,5), mientras que 125 presentaron uso significativo (NUS > 20%). El anlisis de agrupamiento evidenci la existencia de dos grupos de herbolarios. Se recomienda complementar este estudio con evaluaciones farmacolgicas y ecolgicas. To characterize the commercial trade of medicinal plants in Caracas, Venezuela, five popular markets and 10 herb stalls were visited. Stall keepers were interviewed to determine which species were being sold and which were their traditional uses. One hundred ninety eight samples were recorded and 164 species from 72 families were identified. Most of these species are cultivated although wild species from the Andes and Guayana have also been commercialized. One hundred twenty different uses of these plants were recorded and categorized according to 18 disease types, especially those associated with digestive system, infectious and parasitic diseases, as well as those related to skin and subcutaneous tissue. Multi-purpose species were dominant (164, IVF > 0,5), while 125 species show significant use (NUS > 20%). The cluster analysis evidences two groups of stalls. A complementary study considering pharmacological and ecological assessments is recommended.
41740984|La eficiencia reproductiva de clones de Pachira quinata fue evaluada bajo condiciones de cultivo en los jardines y huertos Clonales Semilleros de El IREL, Barrancas, estado Barinas, Venezuela. Cuatro variables de eficiencia reproductiva fueron consideradas: aborto de semillas, produccin de semillas por vulo, produccin de frutos por flor y fecundidad relativa, esta ultima expresada como el nmero de semillas viables producidas por vulos por inflorescencia. Cada una de las variables fue determinada para cada clon y luego comparada de acuerdo a la procedencia de los clones (cuatro venezolanas y cuatro centroamericanas). El impacio del porcentaje de semillas abortadas sobre la produccin total de semillas es altamente variable (1,3-29,2%), aunque la mayoria de los valores porcentuales de semillas abortadas por fruto fue inferior a 20%, con un valor promedio de 10,9%. La produccin de semillas por vulo fue inferior a 50% (20,3-49,5%) con un promedio de 33,7 semillas por vulo. La relacin fruto/flor vari entre 7,1 y 50,0%, sin embargo, la mayora de los valores estn alrededor de 20%. La fecundidad relativa vari entre 3,7 a 14,5% (=6,6%). La produccin de frutos por flor y la fecundidad relativa fueron las unicas variables estadisticamente diferentes entre procedencias. De los resultados de la matriz de correlacin destaca que 60,8% de la varianza en la fecundidad es explicada por la produccin de frutos por flor. De acuerdo a informacin de estudios previos, los resultados obtenidos en la eficiencia reproductiva pueden ser asociados a la autoincompatibilidad gentica, limitacin de polinizadores, limitacin de recursos y la vecindad de ramets de los mismos clones en la plantacin. The reproductive efficiency of clones of Pachira quinata was evaluated under cultivation conditions in the garden and seed clonal orchards at El IREL, Barrancas, State Barinas, Venezuela. Four variables of reproductive efficiency were considered: abortion of seeds, production of seeds by ovule, production of fruits by flower and the relative fecundity, which is expressed as the number of good seeds produced by ovule by inflorescence. Each one of these variables was determined for each clone and then compared according to the origin of the clones (four of Venezuelan origin and four of Central American origin). The percentage of seeds aborted by fruit shows that the impact on the total production of seed set is highly variable (1.3-29.2%), although most of the percentage values of seeds aborted by fruit were inferior to 20%, with an average value of 10.9%. The production of seeds by ovule was from 20.3 to 49.5% with an average of33.7% seeds per ovule. The relation fruit/flower was low and varied between 7.1 and 50.0%, nevertheless, most values of fruit production were around 20%. The relative fecundity varied from 3.7 to 14.5%, averaging 6.61%. The production of fruits per flower and the relative fecundity were the only reproductive variables statistically different among clone origins. According to the results of correlation matrix, 60.8% of the variance in the fecundity is explained by the production of fruits per flower. According to the information of previous studies, the results obtained in the reproductive efficiency may be associated to the genetic self incompatibility, pollinator limitation, resource limitation and the neighborhood of ramets of the same clones in the plantation.

41740431|1) En el desarrollo del aparato estomtico se reconocen dos tipos principales: el tipo perigneo de las clulas auxiliares en el cual las clulas acompaantes se originan de clulas epidrmicas vecinas a la clula madre de las oclusivas y el tipo mesogneo en el cual se forman tanto las clulas acompaantes como las oclusivas de la misma clula madre 2) El tipo perigneo encontrado principalmente en las monocotiledneas (Gramneas, Commelinaceae, Palmae, Marantaqeae, Musaceae etc.) se divide en cuatro subtipos: a) El subtipo de Saccharum, comn de la mayora de las gramineae, en el cual las clulas acompaantes se inician en clulas epidrmicas de dos diferentes hileras celulares adyacentes a la hilera de la cual procede la clula madre de las oclusivas. b) El subtipo de Pariana en el cual se forman tambin dos clulas acompaantes que proceden de la clula epidrmica superior e inferior adyacentes a la clula madre de las oclusivas, es decir que se forman de la misma hilera celular que el estoma el cual est dispuesto perpendicular a las hileras longitudinales de clulas epidrmicas. c) El subtipo de Rhoeo discolor y de las Commelinaceae en general en el cual se forman cuatro clulas acompaantes de cuatro diferentes clulas epidrmicas adyacentes a la clula madre de las oclusivas (dos laterales, una superior y una inferior). d) Por ltimo, el subtipo actinoctico que es caracterstico de las dicotiledneas; el nmero de clulas acompaantes puede variar entre dos y seis. b) El subtipo perpendicular o transversal en el cual la clula madre se divide de la misma manera que en a), pero el poro est perpendicular al eje divisorio de las clulas acompaantes (en vez de paralelamente como en a), ya que en la ltima divisin que da origen a las dos clulas oclusivas el eje divisorio da una vuelta de 90. Por lo tanto, consideramos el subtipo lateral-paralelo y el subtipo perpendicular como dos variaciones de la misma forma fundamental. c) El subtipo espiral, realizado p. e. en Sedum en el cual la clula madre triangular forma segmentos sucesivamente a lo largo de las tres caras siguiendo un espiral; el modo de divisin es comparable al mismo de una clula inicial que se divide a tres caras. Como caso deducido del subtipo espiral consideramos la forma con tres clulas acompaantes que rodean a la clula madre de las oclusivas; se supone que se trata de una reduccin del nmero de las clulas acompaantes. d) El suptipo irregular en el cual se inician las clulas acompaantes de la misma clula madre que las oclusivas, pero el nmero de las clulas acompaantes, su disposicin y el modo de dividirse de la clula madre es indefinido. 4) Los tiops de desarrollo hallados por nosotras coinciden muy bien con los tipos establecidos a base de la forma adulta del aparato estomtico. El tipo de Saccharum coincide con el tipo de las gramneas de Stebbins & Khush. El tipo de Rhoeo discolor coincide con los dos tipos de cuatro o ms clulas acompaantes (Rhoco, palmae) de Stebbins y Khush. El tipo lateral-paralelo coincide con el tipo paractico de Metcalfe & Chalk; el tipo perpendicular o transversal coincide con el tipo diactico de Mefcalfe & Chalk; el tipo espiral coincide con el tipo anisoctico de Metcalfe & Chalk; y el tipo irregular coincide ms o menos con el tipo anomictico de Metcalfe & Chalk. 5) Las divisiones desiguales (Bnning 1953) son muy comunes en la formacin de las clulas acompaantes, especialmente de las Graminaeae, Commelinaceae y otras monocotiledneas.

41740937|El presente trabajo es una revisin bibliogrfica sobre los aspectos etnobotnicos de la palma Mauritia flexuosa L. f en la Cuenca Amaznica, con especial nfasis en Venezuela, apoyado con actividades de herbario y de campo. Nuestras investigaciones revelan que el moriche es un recurso forestal no maderable subutilizado con un gran potencial econmico. Si bien esta especie tiene una amplia distribucin en Amrica tropical, slo los Warao del Delta del Orinoco y los criollos han aprendido a explotarla eficientemente para satisfacer sus mltiples necesidades. Visitas y entrevistas realizadas en los mercados, comercios y centros tursticos en los estados Amazonas, Delta Amacuro, Gurico y Monagas, muestran que los frutos y hojas, as como los productos derivados de stos, son muy cotizados por los turistas y poblacin local, generando fuentes de ingresos adicionales al ncleo familiar. A pesar de la importancia ecolgica y valor cultural de las comunidades de morichal, poco se conoce sobre la morfologa de la especie, estrategias de regeneracin y estado de conservacin de las poblaciones naturales, las cuales son susceptibles de ser afectadas por actividades relacionadas con la explotacin petrolera y agroindustrial, as como por quema, tala y extraccin indiscriminada de sus hojas con fines lucrativos. Supported by herbarium as well as fieldwork, this present paper represents a bibliographical revision of the ethnobotanical aspects of the moriche palm (Mauritia flexuosa) in the Amazon Basin with a particular emphasis on Venezuela. Our investigations show that the moriche is an underdeveloped, non-lumber, forest resource of great economic potential. Although the species is widely distributed in tropical America, only the Warao of the Orinoco Delta and certain Creole populations have learned to efficiently exploit the palm to satisfy multiple needs. In situ inquiries were made among the markets, stores and tourist center in the Venezuelan states of Amazonas, Delta Amacuro, Gurico and Monagas. The resulting data demostrates that the fruit and leaves, as well as their byproducts, are not only valued by tourists and the local population alike, but they also generate an important revenue for the nuclear family. In spite of the ecological and cultural importance of the moriche groves, little is known about their morphology, regeneration strategies and the actual conditions of existing natural groves. Also addressed is the susceptibility of this species to petroleum, agroindustrial and swidden activities as well as the effects of indiscriminate harvesting of its leaves for lucrative ends.

41740530|Se describe un nuevo mtodo para medir granos de polen al microscopio ptico, extensible a cualquier otro tipo de estructuras analizadas por esta va. Empleando un microscopio con cmara clara, una lmina para calibracin de oculares y papel milimetrado, se elabora un instrumento de medida micrometrado, es decir, papel milimetrado calibrado en mieras, para cada aumento; con dicho instrumento se medirn los granos luego de haber sido dibujados detalladamente con la cmara clara. Se presentan las ventajas del mtodo y su similitud estadstica con el mtodo tradicional que emplea ocular graduado. A new method to measure pollen grains using light microscope is described. This method may be used to measure any other structure optically analyzed. With the aid of a light microscope equipped with drawing tube (lucid camera), calibrating microslide, and millimetered paper, a micrometered measurement instrument, i.e. millimetered paper calibrated in microns, is made for each magnification. With this instrument, pollen grains and other structures can be measured using a detailed drawing made with the lucid camera. The advantages of this method, as well as its statistical similarity with the traditional method using graduated oculars, are presented.
41740730|Este trabajo tuvo por objetivo estimar y comparar los cambios de la vegetacin y de la superficie de agua en Laguna Grande (Estado Monagas) durante 45 aos (1947-1992). Se realiz fotointerpretacin de fotografas areas de los aos 1947,1969,1982 y 1992. Durante 1992 se identificaron los siguientes tipos de vegetacin en la laguna y sus alrededores: bosque siempreverde estacionalmente inundado, bosque siempreverde de pantano, pantanos herbceos compuestos por Cyperaceae y Poaceae, pantanos herbceos dominados por Montrichardia arborescens y comunidades de plantas flotantes libres. En los pantanos herbceos se hicieron mustreos de la vegetacin y del banco de semillas. En las unidades boscosas se realizaron descripciones generales y se identificaron las especies ms importantes. La fotointerpretacin y planimetra dio como resultado que en 1947 la cobertura boscosa representaba el 35,7%, y para 1992 el 12,7% del rea total (1667 ha). La superficie del cuerpo de agua, comparando con 1947, ha disminuido en 28%. Con el incremento de las actividades antrpicas en la zona, al menos desde 1969, adems de la reduccin de la cobertura boscosa, se ha presentado eutrofizacin de la laguna, desaparicin de plantas sumergidas y flotantes arraigadas, y una gran parte de la superficie del agua ha sido cubierta por Eichhornia crassipes y Pistia stratiotes. Las orillas arenosas han sido ocupadas por pantanos leosos (bosque siempreverde de pantano) y por pantanos herbceos dominados por M. arborescens. La comparacin entre los pantanos herbceos permite suponer que ha ocurrido un proceso sucesional desde los humedales herbceos compuestos por Cyperaceae y Poaceae hacia los dominados por M. arborescens. In this work we estimate and compare changes in vegetation and water surface of Laguna Grande (Monagas State, Venezuela) during a 45 year period (1947-1992). Photointerpretationof airphotographs of the years 1947, 1969, 1982 and 1992 was carried out. During 1992 the following units of vegetation were identified in the lake and its surroundings: evergreen seasonally flooded forest, swamp forest, marshes dominated by Cyperaceae and Poaceae, herbaceous swamp dominated by Montrichardia arborescens and communities of free-floating hydrophytes. In the herbaceous wetlands sampling of the vegetation and seed bank were carried out. In the wooded units general descriptions were carried out and the most important species were identified. Photointerpretation and planimetry techniques showed that in 1947 the evergreen seasonally flooded forest had 35.7% and in 1992 12.7% of the total area (1667 ha). The water surface of the lake, as compared to 1947, has decreased by 28%. The increase in anthropic activities in the zone, at least since 1969, and the reduction of the woody cover, has occurred eutrophication of the lake. Furthermore, submerged and floating-leaved hydrophytes disappeared, and Eichhornia crassipes and Fistia stratiotes have covered a large part of the water body. The sandy shore has been covered by a swamp forest, and communities dominated by M. arborescens. The comparison between the herbaceous wetlands allow us to suppose that a succession from marshes dominated by Cyperaceae and Poaceae toward a communities dominated by M. arborescens has occurred.

As a conclusion Oritrophium has a disjunct distribution between North America and South America, with higher number of species and a higher endemism in Ecuador, Per and Venezuela.

41740803|Las caractersticas florales y la estrategia reproductiva de Solanum gardneri Sendth., un arbusto ampliamente distribuido en Venezuela, fueron analizadas considerando el dimorfismo floral asociado a la longitud del estilo con el objeto de establecer si esta condicin floral determina un sistema sexual andromonoico. Las flores ofrecen polen como nica recompensa, presentan una antesis diurna y los polinizadores fueron abejas pertenecientes a los gneros Augochloropsis, Centris, Exomalopsis y Xylocopa. El sistema de apareamiento es la xenogamia, caracterstico de especies autoincompatibles, asociado con una alta relacin Polen/vulo y una alta asignacin de biomasa masculina y de atraccin. La esterilidad femenina del morfo floral con estilo corto, unida a diferencias significativas entre los morfos florales en cuanto al nmero y tamao de los vulos, as como en el tamao de los granos de polen, indica la condicin funcionalmente andromonoica de S. gardneri. La hiptesis de la funcin masculina parece explicar la produccin relativamente alta de frutos. El alto nivel de aborto de vulos encontrado se ha asociado con una mejor utilizacin de los recursos a nivel postcigtico y al elevado nmero de semillas por fruto, lo que probablemente est relacionado con la estrategia de diseminacin, siendo la ornitocoria el mecanismo de dispersin encontrado. The breeding system and floral characteristics of Solanum gardneri Sendth., a woody shrub widely distributed in Venezuela, were investigated considering the floral dimorphism associated with the pistil length in order to know if this floral condition determi Anthesis is diurnal; flowers offering only pollen as reward, and the pollinators are bees, belonging to the genera Augochloropsis, Centris, Exomalopsis and Xylocopa. S. gardneri has a xenogamous mating system, of a self-incompatible species, related to a high P/O ratio, associated with a high biomass allocation to male and attraction functions. Female sterility in short-style flower and significant differences between floral morphs in number and ovule size, and pollen size indicate the andromonocious condition of S. gardneri. The allocation invested in the male function and in the attraction structures promote outcrossing. The male function explains the relatively high fruit-set. The high ovule abortion level found has been associated to a better postcigotic resource allocation level and the higher seed number per fruit is probably related to the fruit dispersal strategy, which is ornitochory.

41740712|Se describe la estructura y composicin floristica, as como las distribuciones geogrficas de las especies encontradas en tres tipos de bosque hmedo tropical situados en la cuenca baja del Rio Caura, Edo. Bolvar, Venezuela. Se documentaron 3719 rboles >=10 cm de dimetro en 62 parcelas de vegetacin de 0,1 heetrea, informatin que se utilizo para clasificar bosques de terra firme, bosques ocasionalmente inundados a lo largo de caos y bosques estacionalmente inundados a lo largo del ro. Los bosques de terra firme del bajo Caura tenan relativamente baja densidad de rboles grandes (>=50 cm DAP), baja rea basal (promedio de 22,3 m/ha), elevada riqueza de especies (promedio de 137 spp./ha) y no estaban dominados por ninguna especie (IVmax=13,92 de 300). Los bosques estacionalmente inundados a lo largo del rio tenan la densidad mas alta de rboles pequeos (<20 cm DAP), los rboles mas grandes documentados durante ese estudio (DAP -120 cm), fueron los mas pobres en especies (promedio de 82 spp./ha). Los bosques ocasionalmente inundados a lo largo de caos tenan caracteristicas intermedias. Ambos tipos de bosques inundados estaban mas dominados por ciertas especies (IVmax/L= 22,76 y 23,07 de 300) y tenan reas basales mayores (promedio de 25,5 y 26,8 m/ha) que los bosques de terra firme. Las familias Leguminosae (s.l.) y Lecythidaceae tenan los valores de importancia mayores en los tres tipos de bosque y la mayora de las especies botnicamente identificadas tenan una amplia distribucin geogrfica neotropical. Por lo menos dos especies documentadas en el bajo Caura estn actualmente consideradas como endmicas de la Guayana de Venezuela. A causa de sus caractersticas estructurales y florsticas, los bosques del bajo Caura no son interesantes para la explotacin de madera a gran escala basada en la tala de pocas especies comerciales. This paper describes the structure, floristic composition and floristic affinities of the three main forest types found in a lowland rain forest in the Caura watershed, Edo. Bolvar, Venezuela. We inventoried 3719 trees above 10 cm diameter at breast height in 62 vegetation plots of 0.1 hectare representing closed-canopy terra firme forest, sporadically flooded forest near small streams and seasonally flooded riparian forest. The terra firme forest of the lower Caura was characterized by comparatively low density of big trees (>= 50 cm DBH), low overall basal area (average of 22.3 m/ha), high species richness (average of 137 spp./ha), and low degree of dominance by any one species (maximum IV = 13.92 of 300). The seasonally flooded forest had the highest density of small trees (<20 cm DBH), the largest trees (110 to 120 cm DBH) documented during this study, and the lowest species richness (average of 82 spp./ha). The sporadically flooded forest was intermediate in most traits. Both flooded forest types had higher degrees of dominance by a single species (max. IV = 22.76 and 23.07 of 300) and higher basal areas (average 25.5 and 26.8 m/ha.) than the terra firme forest. Leguminosae (s.l.) and Lecythidaceae had the highest family importance values in all three forest types and the majority of species that could be identified had a wide neotropical distribution, but we also documented at least two species currently considered endemic to Venezuelan Guayana. Because of their structural and floristic characteristics, the forests of the lower Caura are unattractive for large-scale timber exploitation based on selective cutting of a few commercial species.

Naudin es un arbusto de amplia distribucin en los andes sudamericanos, pese a ello, los estudios de la especie se limitan a escasos trabajos morfolgicos y florsticos. Monochaetum meridense (H. Karst.) Naudin is a widely distributed shrub of the South American Andes, however, the studies carried out for this species are restricted to a few morphological descriptions and floristic surveys. 41740752|El objetivo del presente trabajo es verificar la existencia de anormalidades cromosmicas asociadas a la baja fertilidad del polen en Aloe vera. El estudio se realiz a partir del aplastamiento de anteras inmaduras fijadas en etanol-actico y coloreadas con orceina. La viabilidad del polen se determin en microcultivos de agar y sacarosa. Las anormalidades ms frecuentes en meiosis I fueron: quiasmas persistentes entre homlogos grandes y desplazamiento precoz de cromosomas pequeos, uno ms puentes dicntricos solitarios acompaados con fragmentos acntricos. En meiosis II, se observ la presencia ocasional de puentes y fragmentos, adems de microsporas adicionales en la etapa de ttradas. Rupturas cromosmicas, errores de entrecruzamiento e inversion paracntrica heterocigtica entre homlogos de mayor tamao se discuten como posibles causas de las irregularidades meiticas observadas. The objective of this work is to verify the existence of chromosomic abnormalities associated to the low fertility of pollen in Aloe vera. The study was carried out starting from the squashing of immature anthers fixed in acetic-ethanol and stained with orceine. The viability of the pollen was determined in agar and sucrose microculture. The most frequent abnormalities in meiosis I were: chiasmata not finished between big homologous, and precocious displacement of small chromosomes, one or more solitary or accompanied dicentric bridges with acentric fragments. In meiosis II, the occasional presence of bridges and fragments was observed, just as additional microspores. Chromosome breakage, crossing-over errors and heterozygotic paracentric inversion between greatest homologous are discussed like possible causes of the observed meiotic irregularities.

La altura media de los culmos vari entre 1,40 y 1,80 m, con su valor ms alto cuando la profundidad fue mayor. La densidad media de culmos fue 35 culmos/m 2 , y vari entre 23 y 45 culmos/m, con los valores ms altos durante el primer perodo lluvioso. La media de la biomasa total fue de 1015351 g seco/m y vari entre 310 y 1465 g seco/m con el valor ms bajo en diciembre (segundo perodo de lluvias), y el ms alto en agosto (primer perodo de lluvias). Hymenachne amplexicaulis (Poaceae) is a robust, rhizomatous perennial grass; it forms dense monospecific colonies in seasonally flooded environments and along riverbanks in tropical and subtropical wetlands of America. The objective of this study was to determine the effects of seasonal variations of water depth on the growth, above ground biomass and production of H, amplexicaulis in a freshwater marsh situated in Miranda State (Venezuela) between February and December 2001. H. amplexicaulis showed variations in the biomtrie characteristics, such as height, length of internode, density of culms related to changes of water depth. The mean height of culms varied between 1.4 and 1.8 m, with the highest value in deep water. Mean density of culms was 35 culm/m and ranged between 24 y 49 culms/m, with the highest values during the first rain period (August). Mean total biomass was 1015351 dry g/m and varied between 310 and 1465 dry g/m, with the lowest value during the second rain period (December) and the highest value during the the first rain period. Flowering and fructification began in October and finished in February; inflorescence biomass, including flowers and fruits, ranged between 1.4 and 14.9 dry g/m, and it represented less than 1% of total biomass. The annual net primary production was of 822 dry g/m/year. H. amplexicaulis tolerate continual flood conditions, but in deep water there was a significative decreasing in the total biomass and their components (leaf, culms, standing dead material and inflorescences), which may indicate limitations of gaseous interchange and nutrient uptake.

Total nitrogen was lower on December and higher on August. Net absorption and N-use efficiency of leaves and stems showed different behaviors study period. Seasonal changes of water depth influenced concentration, absorption and nitrogen-use efficiency by the grass H. amplexicaulis.

This document was focused on: the compilation of basic documentary information about the species of Oritrophium described in Venezuela; information about the species known as frailejn morado, and the mechanisms of its commercialization; information about its collection in the Andean Pramo by local people; verification in situ of the state of these species in a series of selected locations; and characterization of the habitat and requirements of frailejn morado. In the light of the information collected, frailejn morado corresponds only to Oritrophium peruvianum, but not to O. venezuelense. O. peruvianum is known and collected in mountain communities; part of the gathered material is kept for domestic use and a certain volume for regional commercialization.

All floral traits differed according to clone origin. Floral external diameter, diameter of floral tube, floral length, and herkogamy were larger for South American clones, and floral internal diameter and flower tube length were larger for Central American clones. Morphometrical floral traits allow us to discriminate between geographical origins of clones. However, there is a broad range of variation, since only 65% of flowers were properly classified according geographical locality. A second discriminant analysis, using morphological traits, showed significant differences between South and Central American flowers. In order of importance, floral traits that allow discrimination between geographic areas are as follows: 1. hercogamy, 2. external diameter, 3. tube length, and 4. internal diameter. These traits correctly discriminated a high percentage (86.9%) of flowers according to geographic origin. Morphometrical variations of floral traits are discussed in relation to its breeding system, pollination mode and geographical distribution.

41740988|El presente trabajo tuvo por objeto tipificar los procesos de megasporognesis y megagametognesis en Hymenocallis caribaea y algunos caracteres de su desarrollo seminal. Para elio, se sigui la metodologa anatmica sugerida por Johansen (1940) en estudios embriolgicos. Los vulos de H. caribaea son bitgmicos y pseudocrasinucelados. El tegumento externo se mantiene indiferenciado hasta la etapa postfertilizacin y se encuentra profusamente vascularizado. El micrpilo se forma en zig-zag con la intervencin de ambos tegumentos que se encuentran desalineados, carcter considerado evolutivamente primitivo. La meiosis se produce mientras la yema floral est completamente inmersa en el bulbo. La clula madre de las megsporas proviene directamente del megasporocito, del cual se forman cuatro megsporas reducidas y slo la situada en el polo calazal se mantiene funcional (megasporognesis monosprica), dando origen al saco embrionario. La megagametognesis sigue un patrn del tipo Polygonum, con ocho clulas en el saco embrionario maduro: tres clulas micropilares (dos sinrgidas y una ovoclula), tres calazales (antpodas) y dos ncleos polares en el centro-lateral del saco embrionario. Espordicamente se produce ms de un saco embrionario por vulo, pero stos no parecen culminar con la formacin de ms de un embrin por semilla. El desarrollo y diferenciacin del vulo de H. caribaea para formar una semilla verde, carnosa, con baja relacin peso/volumen, profusamente vascularizada, con embrin rudimentario hasta bien adelantado su desarrollo y a veces vivpara, parece reflejar una adaptacin al medio particular donde se desarrollan estas plantas. The main objective of the present research was to characterize the processes of megasporogenesis and megagametogenesis in Hymenocallis caribaea and some characteristics of its seed development. To achieve it, there were followed the anatomical methodology suggested by Johansen (1940) for embryological purposes. Ovules of H. caribaea are bitegmic and pseudocrassinucelate. Outer integument rests undifferentiated until the postfertilization stage and it is profusely vascularized. Both integuments form a zig-zag micropile, which is considered evolutionarily primitive. Meiosis occurs while flower buds are completely immersed in the bulb. Megaspore mother cell origins directly from megasporocite. During megasporogenesis four megaspores are formed and only the one at the chalazal pole remains functional (monosporic type), giving rise to the embryo sac. Megagametogenesis follows the Polygonum pattern, with eight cells in the mature embryo sac: three micropilar cells (two sinergids and the egg cell), three chalazal cells (antipodes), and two polar nuclei in the center-side of the embryo sac. More than one embryo sac per ovule sporadically occurs, but they do not appear to lead to the formation of more than one embryo per seed. Development and differentiation of the ovule of H. caribaea to form a green, fleshy, low weight/volume, profusely vascularized seed, with a rudimentary embryo until its development is well advanced, appears to reflect an adaptation to the particular environment where these plants grow.

41740845|Se estudi la biologa reproductiva de Amasonia campestris en los Altos Llanos Centrales venezolanos. Las flores abren entre las 3:30 y las 7:00 h, con una longevidad de dos dias. Las flores son protandras, y el nmero de flores abiertas por inflorescencias por dia varia de 1 a 5 ($\bar X$ = 2,2, DS = 2,3). El nctar es producido y acumulado en la cavidad basai de la corola. La secrecin de nctar comienza a las 7:00 y se prolonga hasta las 13:00 h, El volumen total de nctar por flor durante los dos dias de actividad floral vari entre 8,55 y 35,15 ml/flor, con una media de 21,75 ml (DS = 9,19). Las flores de A. campestris son visitadas por cuatro especies de mariposas de la familia Pieridae y tres especies de colibres. La actividad de los colibres fue mayor en horas de la maana y de la tarde y las visitas de las mariposas fueron mucho ms frecuentes en horas del medio da independientemente de la densidad de plantas, aunque la tasa de visitas de mariposas y colibres fue estadisticamente mayor a alta densidad de plantas. El patrn de produccin de nctar est positivamente correlacionado con la tasa de visitas de los colibres Amazilia fimbriata obscuricauda (n = 8, r = 0,95, P<0,0001) y Chlorostilbon mellisuga caribaeus (n = 8, r = 0,73, P<0,02) a alta densidad de plantas. Amasonia campestris produce alto porcentaje de frutos y semillas por polinizacin cruzada comparado con las pruebas de polinizacin automtica y autopolinizacin manual, lo cual indica autoincompatibilidad. Ms del 50% de la biomasa floral es asignada a la corola. La relacin de biomasa reproductiva/biomasa vegetativa fue de 0,37 indicando un desbalance entre esporofilas y pertanto. La relacin polen/vulo fue de 1250. La produccin promedio de frutos por flor fue 64,26% y la produccin de semillas por vulo fue 73,94%. La alta fecundidad relativa (46,72%) en A. campestris parece estar condicionada, principalmente, por la combinacin de cuatro caracteres: eficiencia de polinizacin, bajo nmero de vulos por flor, protandria y forma de vida herbcea perenne. Reproductive biology of Amasonia campestris was studied in the Venezuelan Central Llanos. The flowers open between 3:30 and 7:00 h, and last for two days. The flowers are protandrous and the number of opened flowers per inflorescence varies between 1 and 5 ($\bar X$ = 2.2, SD = 2.3). The nectar is produced and accumulated in a basal cavity of the corolla. Nectar secretion begins at 7:00 and finishes at 13:00 h. The total nectar volume produced per flower during two days of longevity was between 8.55 and 35.15 l/flower ($\bar X$ = 21.75 l, SD = 9.19). The flowers were visited by four butterfly (Pieridae) and three hummingbird species. The highest activity of hummingbirds was during the morning and afternoon, and the highest activity of butterflies occurred during the midday at low and high plant density, however, the visits were higher for hummingbirds and butterflies at high plant density. The patterns of nectar secretion were positively correlated with the number of visits of two hummingbirds, Amazilia fimbriata obscuricauda (n = 8, r = 0.95, P<0.0001) and Chlorostilbon mellisuga caribaeus (n = 8, r = 0.73, P<0.02) at high plant density. Fruit and seed set in cross-pollinated flowers were higher than hand self-pollination and spontaneous self-pollination respectively, which suggest self-incompatibility. More than 50% of floral biomass is allocated to the corolla. Reproductive/vegetative biomass ratio was 0.37, which indicate an unbalanced between sporophyll and perianth. Pollen/ovule ratio was 1250. Natural fruit set was 64.26% and seed set (relative to ovules) was 73.94%. High value of relative fecundity in A. campe stris seems to be mainly determined by the combination of four traits: pollination efficiency, low number of ovules per flower, protandry, and perennial herbaceous life form.

Las flores de T. paniculatum son actinomorfas, pequeas, amarillas, y con una longevidad floral de cuatro horas, caractersticas que concuerdan con el tipo y tamao de los visitantes florales, los cuales fueron principalmente abejas de diferentes familias (Apidae y Halictidae). La carga de polen depositada naturalmente sobre los estigmas fue 2.94 veces mayor que el nmero de vulos por flor y el porcentaje de granos de polen germinados fue bajo (24,9%). La produccin natural de frutos por flor y semillas por vulo fue de 60,4% y 86,5%, respecivamente. Los bajos nivels de vulos abortados y la ausencia de semillas abortadas contribuyeron a una produccin de semillas formadas por vulos por inflorescencia relativamente alta (52,3%). T. paniculatum exhibi un sistema de apareamiento con predominancia de autogamia, el cual estaba correlacionado con una baja relacin polen/vulo (136,1), baja asignacin de biomasa masculina pre- (0,39) y post-cigtica (0,03) en la flor y una baja relacin pericarpo/semilla (0,57). La proporcin de frutos y semillas producidos por autofertilizacin fue significativamente mayor que la proporcin producida por fertilizacin cruzada, lo cual sugiere que altos niveles de autogamia pueden estar asociados a una depresin por exogamia que favorece la permanencia de genotipos altamente adaptados a parches de bosques aislados en zonas urbanas. The reproductive biology of Talinum paniculatum (Portulacaceae), a hermaphrodite herb in a remnant of semideciduous forest in Caracas, Venezuela, was studied. Pollination biology, breeding system, and fruit and seed set were determined. The flowers were actinomorphic, yellowish, small, and live for only four hours. These floral traits were correlated with the pollinator types and sizes, which were represented by bees from different families (Apidae and Halictidae). Pollen load deposited naturally on the stigmas was 2.94 times larger than the number of ovule per flower, and the percentage of germination was 24.9%. The natural production of fruit per flower and seed per ovule was 60.4% and 86.5%, respectively. The lowest level of ovule abortion and the absence of seed abortion contributed to the relatively high level of seed produced per ovule per inflorescence (52.3%). T. paniculatum has a mating system biased toward autogamy, which is correlated with a low polen/ovule ratio (136.1), low pre-(0.39) and post-cigotic (0.03) biomass allocation to male function in flower, and a low pericarp/seed ratio (0.57). The proportion of fruit and seed produced by self-pollination was significantly higher than the proportion produced by cross-pollination which suggest that high levels of autogamy may be associated with outbreeding depression, favouring genotypes highly adapted to small forest fragments located in urban areas.

41740633|In the cloud forests of the Cordillera de la Costa de Venezuela at altitudes varying from 800-1500 meters there is to be found a small part of the flora definitely showing a Guayana and/or Amazonian relationship. In some cases the element of the flora involves the same species, in other cases the element is that of related species of the same genus. This Amazonian-Guayanan element manifests itself in the Coastal Cordillera cloud forests either as rare isolated outposts of endemism (Froesia, Macrocentrum, Elvasia) or as more widespread in their distribution in the Coastal Cordillera (Mapania pycnocephala subsp. fluviatilis, Vriesea splendens var. splendens). In the latter cases, the distribution of the species in the Coastal Cordillera may range from Estado Yaracuy on the west to Estado Sucre on the East in the Pennsula de Paria. This element of the Amazonian-Guayanan flora present in the cloud forested upper elevations of the Coastal Cordillera is mainly absent in the Andes. This difference is explained by the relatively older Coastal Cordillera and its different geological history and connections with the Guayana Shield. It is postulated that the Amazonian-Guayanan portion of the Coastal Cordillera flora represents an ancient relict flora which has survived only on the upper levels of the Coastal Cordillera as a result of adaptation to progressive elevations of the Guayana Shield in past geological epochs, whereas the absence of this element from the lower levels of the Coastal Cordillera is due to its destruction by both inundations and elevations.

Por el desdoblamiento de los mrgenes hacia atrs se forma una hoja enrollada con una cripta que representa un espacio al abrigo del viento. Dentro de la cripta se encuentran los estomas, por lo cual se reduce la transpiracin considerablemente. La estructura de la hoja es sumamente xeromorfa, es decir, adaptada al clima adversario de los pramos con sequa, fro, calor, viento y fuertes cambios de temperatura. El desarrollo de la hoja coincide con el descrito por Hagerup (1953) en ciertas ericceas. The needle shaped leaf of Hinterhubera imbricata shows the ericoid structure typical of certain ericaceae. By turning backwards of the leaf margins a rolled leaf is formed with a crypt in which the stomata develop; transpiration is thus reduced considerably. The xeromorphic structure of the leaf is very adequate to the hostile climate of the "paramos" in which plants are exposed to extreme dryness, abrupt changes of heat and frost, wind etc. The development of the leaf coincides with that of certain ericaceae studied by Hagerup (1953). The original leaf margins cease to grow early in development, whereas secondary margins are formed on the lower side of the leaf close to the extremities. In Hinterhubera a false rolled leaf is therefore represented. Longitudinally, se leaf subdivides into a apical part which is reduced in its width as well as in the differentiation of the mesophyll; a well developed middle part with an anatomical structure characteristic of the ericoid leaf; and a basal part without rolled margins, adapted to its supporting function by development of mechanical tissue (fibers); in this part stomata are lacking as well as glands and hairs and no differentiation of the mesophyll into palisade parenchyma and spongy parenchyma takes place. A petiole is missing. It surprises that the leaf of a species of the compositae imitates completely the rolled leaf of certain ericaceae in its anatomy as well as in its development; as this ericoid type of leaf is found also in several other species pertaining to different families, it may represent a special adaptation to the unfavourable climate of the paramos in the Andes, fafalsrolledleafd

The character analysis has evidenced the presence in the country of taxa with tetra-or bi-sporing anthers, and fruits with and without pappus. The first chromosome counting is presented here for the species V. laurifolia (n=32). Pollen grains are classified by size and by exin sculturations in six groups, one of them new for the genus. The results are analyzed from the taxonomical as well as from the possible evolutionary relationships. A bibliographic summary of its therapeutical importance is included.

43957304|En xerfitas, los rasgos anatmicos particulares desarrollados para la supervivencia y adaptacin en un medio donde los recursos hdricos y minrales son limitantes, son llamados caracteres xeromorfos y entre stos se encuentran: cuticula gruesa, paredes celulares engrosadas, alta densidad de tricomas muertos, estomas abundantes y hundidos en la epidermis, etc. Se estudi la epidermis foliar de Jacquinia armillaris (Primulaceae), Capparis flexuosa (Capparaceae), Quadrella odoratissima (Capparaceae) y Erithalis fruticosa (Rubiaceae), cuatro especies siempreverdes de la isla La Tortuga (Venezuela), con el fin de analizar los rasgos anatmicos epidrmicos con potencial valor adaptativo al ambiente xrico tipico de esta isla, cuya vegetacin ha sido estudiada hasta ahora slo desde el punto de vista taxonmico. Las hojas seleccionadas de cada especie fueron procesadas para su anlisis en vista superficial, a travs de la tcnica de extraccin epidrmica, y en vista transversal, mediante cortes transversales de la lamina foliar. Los rasgos anatmicos adaptativos observados fueron: cutcula gruesa, bajo espesor epidrmico, paredes celulares engrosadas y cristales abundantes en todas las especies examinadas y estomas pequeos, hundidos y abundantes en C. flexuosa y Q. odoratissima. Taies rasgos son tipicos de xerfitas y constituyen posibles adaptaciones de las especies estudiadas a las condiciones ambientales de la isla La Tortuga. In xerophytes, the particular anatomical traits developed to adaptation and survive in environmental conditions of limited hydric and mineral resources, are known as xeromorphyc characters and among these are: thick cuticle, thick cell walls, high density of dead trichomes, numerous and sunken stornata, etc. The leaf epidermis of Jacquinia armillaris (Primulaceae), Capparis flexuosa (Capparaceae), Quadrella odoratissima (Capparaceae) & Erithalis fruticosa (Rubiaceae), four common evergreen species from La Tortuga island (Venezuela), was studied with the objective of analyzing the anatomical traits with potential adaptive values to typical xeric environment of this island, whose vegetation until now has been only studied from the taxonomic point of view. For this reason, the selected leaves of each specie were processed and analyzed in superficial view following the Ram & Nayyar (1974) technique and in cross view, by cross sections of the leaf lamina. The observed adaptive anatomical traits were: thick cuticle, low epidermal thickness, thick cell walls and abundant crystals in all the examined species, and frequent sunken and small stornata in C. flexuosa and Q. odoratissima. Those characters are considered typical of xerophytes and constitute potential adaptations to environmental conditions of La Tortuga island.

41740647|Las hojas de las passifloraceae estudiadas forman variaciones de un cierto tipo fundamental que representa la hoja trifoliolada de Passiflora suberosa con tres pinnas bien desarrolladas. De all se deduce la hoja simple de Passiflora kahlbreyeri con tres nervios principales fuertes por reduccin completa de las pinnas y, al otro lado, se deduce tambin la forma amariposada de Passiflora cuneata por reduccin total de la pinna terminal. En la hoja de las passifloracea se conocen tres tipos diferentes de glndulas: la en forma de protuberancia en el pecolo, la glndula en forma de "Ventana" sobre la lmina y la en forma de tentculo en los ltimos segmentos de las brcteas. La lmina de Passiflora cuneata tiene una epidermis superior de clulas relativamente grandes, un parnquima en empalizada con clulas en forma de embudo, varias capas de parnquima en empalizada con clulas en forma de embudo, varias capas de parnquima esponjoso y una epidermis inferior con clulas en forma de cristal de reloj y con estomas. En los lugares donde se forman las glndulas no se desarrollan parnquima en empalizada ni estomas, ya que la epidermis inferior se transforma en epitelio glandular. Las glndulas se originan por alargamiento anticlinal de las clulas de la epidermis inferior y siguientes divisiones periclinales formndose de esta manera hileras anticlinales de 10 y ms clulas. Las clulas secretoras tienen membrans delgadas, son ricas en protoplasma y sustancias secretoras y no dejan espacios intercelulares entre s. La primera capa subepidrmica muestra tambin divisiones periclinales; sus clulas llevan frecuentemente cristales de oxalato de calcio en forma de drusas. Sobre esta capa se encuentran traqueidas con engrosamientos helicoidales que abastecen las glndulas con agua y sustancias solubles en l. The studied leaves of passifloraceae form variations of a certain fundamental type which is represented by the trifoliolate leave of Passiflora suberosa with 3 well developed leaflets. From this type, the simple leaf of Passiflora kahlbreyeri with 3 main veins can be deduced by complete reduction of the leaflets, and the butterfly shaped leaf of Passiflora cuneata by total reduction of the terminal leaflet. Three different types of glands can be distinguished in the leaf of passifloraceae: one in form of a protuberance at the petiole, an other in form of a "window'' at the leaf blade and a third in form of a tentacle at the end of the segments of the bracts. The blade of Passiflora cuneata has an upper epidermis with relatively large cells, a palisade parenchyma with cells in form of a funnel, several layers of spongy parenchyma and a lower epidermis with cells in form of a watch glass and with stomata. At the level where the glands form, neither palisade parenchyma nor stomata are developed, as the whole lower epidermis transforms into the glandular epithelium. The glands originate by cell enlargement in anticlinal direction and subsequent periclinal divisions from the lower epidermis; in this way anticlinal rows of 10 and more cells are formed. The secretory cells show thin walls, are rich in protoplasm and certain secretory substances and do not leave intercellular spaces between them. The first subepidermal layer shows also periclinal cell divisions; the cells contain frequently crystals of calcium ovlate in form of druses. Above this layer, tracheary elements are found with helicoidal wall thickenings which supply the glands with water and water soluble substances.

The swamp forest (Chaguaramal) located in the northwest border of the Turupano National Park (Sucre State), contains a rich fauna of value for conservation including a variety of parrots, macaws and monkeys, nevertheless the vegetation is little known in Venezuela. The structure of the ligneous vegetation ( 2,5 cm DBH) was studied in four rectangular plots (0.1 ha) and the local flora was inventoried. The dominant arboreal species are Pterocarpus officinalis, Inga vera, Tabebuia rosea, Roystonea oleracea, Ficus maxima, and the herbaceous Montrichardia arborescens, Crinum erubescens and Typha dominguensis. The plants are grouped in three strata and the coverage is, in general, dense in the understory and open in the canopy. Forty three families, 48 genera and 75 species were identified and a species key is presented. The frequent fires in the herbaceous swamps of Eleocharis spp. and Typha dominguensis surrounding the formation constitute a strong threat for the flora and fauna of the Chaguaramal, therefore, its inclusion into the Turupano National Park is recommended to assure its conservation.

41740630|1. El fruto del merey representa un fruto doble compuesto de una baya falsa y de una nuez. La nuez corresponde al fruto verdadero que procede del gineceo y contiene la nica semilla, mientras que la baya falsa se origina del pednculo de la flor. 2. La pared del ovario se compone de una protodermis externa, un parnquima perifrico de varias capas, un anillo de procambium, y un parnquima interno que est cubierto por la protodermis interna. 3. El anillo de cavidades secretoras se forma algo ms tarde y las mismas cavidades se originan de manera esquizgena. 4. La pared del ovario muestra un crecimiento en circunferencia muy pronunciado al cual se adapta la epidermis externa por divisiones anticlinales, mientras que las clulas del parnquima externo e interno se estiran tangencialmente y luego se dividen anticlinalmente. 5. El procambium se diferencia relativamente tarde y se transforma en un anillo irregular compuesto de un gran nmero de haces vasculares. 6. El crecimiento en anchura del pericarpio es moderado y se promueve principalmente por el ensanchamiento de las cavidades secretoras que en estado maduro del fruto ocupan una parte considerable; aumentan de tamao tanto por divisiones anticlinales de las clulas parenquimticas que las rodean como por el estiramiento radial de las clulas parenquimticas que forman los tabiques separadores anticlinales entre las cavidades. La epidermis interna se hace de esta manera "pluriestratificada". La primera capa subepidrmica conserva sus clulas muy pequeas que luego ensanchan tambin sus paredes. Estas dos capas forman el endocarpio del fruto. 8. El parnquima perifrico debajo de la epidermis que corresponde a la corteza primaria se adapta al crecimiento en circunferencia por alargamiento tangencial de sus clulas y siguientes divisiones anticlinales. 12. En estado adulto, las clulas parenquimticas tienen membranas delgadas y vacuolas grandes y representan la parte jugosa carnosa y comestible. De cierto modo contribuyen tambin los haces vasculares al crecimiento en anchura del pednculo por divisiones celulares y aumento de las clulas. Tambin las clulas parenquimticas que rodean los haces vasculares muestran mayor actividad divisoria y se dividen frecuentemente periclinalmente alrededor de los mismos. 13. En el presente trabajo se analiz el cariotipo de zbila utilizando tincin con plata (AgNOR) con la finalidad de determinar la localizacin de las regiones organizadoras del nuclolo (NORs) en los cromosomas de dicha planta. The karyotype of Aloe was studied using silver nitrate staining (AgNOR) in order to determine the location of the nucleolus organizer region (NOR). Terminal NORs were observed on the short arms of the smallest chromosomes (pairs 6 and 7) as well as on chromosomes 1 and 4 in the same position. Dark bands were found in most of chromosomes, especially in pair 4. In order to explain the nature of those segments, three hypothesis are presented and it is also suggested that these bands could be nucleoli derived from heterochromatic region which has been named "Nheterochromatin". It is necessary to apply C-banding in future studies in order to get more information about correlation between C-banding positive regions and NORs localization.
41740894|Las especies del gnero Lantana son conocidas por el alto valor comercial de sus aceites naturales, pero se sabe poco de su respuesta fotosinttica a variables ambientales. El efecto del dficit hdrico sobre la actividad fotosinttica se estudi en tres especies de Lantana: L. caracasana, L. canescens y L. camara, con tratamientos de suspensin del riego. L. caracasana tuvo la mayor asimilacin de carbono durante el perodo de medida y el dficit en la disponibilidad de agua ocasion una disminucin del potencial hdrico, de la fotosntesis y de la conductancia estomtica en las tres especies. Los cambios observados en las variables de fluorescencia, en la eficiencia cuntica aparente y en la fotosntesis a luz saturante, sugieren una regulacin descendente de la actividad fotoqumica del fotosistema II durante el dficit hdrico. En plantas control se observaron pocas diferencias entre especies en la respuesta de la fotosntesis a la concentracin intercelular de CO. La temperatura ptima para la fotosntesis vari entre 25-26C. El efecto del dficit hdrico sobre el intercambio gaseoso de las tres especies fue diferente, siendo L. camara la ms afectada. The species of the Lantana genus are known by the high commercial value of its natural oils, but their photosynthetic response to environmental variables is not well known. To characterize the photosynthetic capacity and establish the effect of water deficit on photosynthesis, plants of three Lantana species (L. caracasana, L. canescens and L. camara) were submitted to water deficit by holding watering. The highest diurnal carbon assimilation was observed in L. caracasana and water deficit caused a decline in water potencial, photosynthesis and stomatal conductance of all species. Changes observed in variable fluorescence, apparent quantum yield and photosynthesis at saturated light, suggested a down regulation of photochemical activity of photosystem II during water deficit. In well irrigated plants, slight differences were observed among species in the photosynthetic response to intercellular CO concentration. Optimum temperature of photosynthesis was within 25-26C. The effect of water deficit on the photosynthetic parameters varied with the species, being L. camara the most affected.

Las clulas entre las dos epidermis se transforman en su mayor parte en clulas ptreas (la capa ''crnea" de los autores) con paredes onduladas. Las clulas de la epidermis interna quedan pequeas. El fruto maduro se puede considerar como cpsula, ya que su pericarpio es seco y relativamente delgado y se rompe al final de la maduracin por fisuras irregulares.

41740432|Se estudiaron tres diferentes tipos de hojas anatmicamente que se distinguen en su consistencia: El tipo "coriceo", el tipo "compacto" y el "membranceo". El tipo "compacto" se distingue por la poca cantidad de esclernquima, la formacin de grandes espacios intercelulares, el espesor mayor de la hoja y membranas ms delgadas del mesfilo. El tipo "membranceo" por fin, sobresale por la ausencia relativa de mecnico (esclernquima), la formacin de grandes espacios intercelulares, la sutileza de la hoja y las membranas delgadas del mesfilo.

41740655|The Sierra de San Luis is a range of mountains in the Estado Falcon, composed mainly of the San Luis limestone of Oligocence age. The area covered by this range extends about 37 kilometers from east to west and about 5-7 kilometers wide in its widest portion. Altitudes range to 1500 meters above sea level. A variety of habitats is found in the area, including upland savannas, doud forests, decidous forests, and deserts on the lower slopes. No geological connection has existed either in the Andes or in the Cordillera de la Costa since the Sierra de San Luis originated at a much later date (Pliocene) than the other principal cordilleras of Venezuela. An examination of the flora reveals 1) a greater relationship with the Cordillera de la Costa than with the Andes, and 2) a marked degree of endemicity. Outside of Venezuela, the greatest affinities of the flora of the Sierra de San Luis are with that 1) of Colombia, and 2) of the West Indies, Mexico, and Central America. Because of the youthful age of the Sierra de San Luis, it is believed that the age of the endemic species is no greater than one million years. The migration of the flora has reached the Sierra de San Luis during the past one million years from various sources, one principal center from the Cordillera de la Costa, the other from Colombia.

41740680|Commelinaceae, despus de Poaceae y Cyperaceae, es la familia de monocotiledneas con mayor nmero de malezas de cultivo; entre ellas, algunas especies de Commelina y Tinantia son hospederas de caros, royas y virus, como Potato Y potyvirus que afecta a Solanum tuberosum. Se realiz un estudio de la anatoma de los rganos vegetativos de representantes de las especies Commelina obliqua y Tinantia erecta que crecen en un cultivo de papas en los Andes de Mrida, para tratar de determinar la existencia de caracteres anatmicos comunes y diferenciales para las especies, as como cuales de estos favorecen su establecimiento en el cultivo y la existencia o no de caracteres que indiquen la presencia de posibles patgenos asociados a ellas. Se encontr que ambas especies poseen hojas anfiestomticas, con epidermis de clulas altas, cutcula delgada, mesofilo compacto bien diferenciado, tallos con abundantes races adventicias, caracteres stos que permiten el comportamiento de malezas. Adems se not un contenido aparentemente plasmodial en las clulas de la vaina vascular que podra estar asociado a la presencia de patgenos. Commelinaceae is, after Poaceae and Cyperaceae, the family of monocotiledons with the greatest number of weeds associated to cultures; among them, some species of Commelina and Tinantia are host for acarus, rust and virus, like the Potato Y potyvirus that affects Solanum tuberosum. In the Andes of Mrida, Commelina obliqua and Tinantia erecta grow like weeds in cultivation of potato. To try to determine the existence of common and differential anatomical characters among them, as well as which anatomical characters favor its establishment in the cultivation, and the existence or not of characters that indicate the presence of possible pathogenic agents associated to them, the anatomy of its vegetative organs was carried out. Both species have amphistomatic leaves, tall epidemical cells, thin cuticle; compact and well defined mesophyll; stem showing abundant adventitious roots; all of those being characters that permit the weed condition. In addition, the parenchyma cells of the bundle sheath seem to be filled with a plasmodium, suggesting infection by pathogens.

Es que la estructura estratificada del floema provoca la formacin de un ritidoma anular. 13) El dibujo de la estratificacin predomina en la mayora de los tejidos de la corteza. 14) La estructura regular de la corteza sugiere la hiptesis de que se trata de un tipo ms desarrollado y ms avanzado desde el punto de vista filogentico. Was die Anatomie der Rinde anbelangt, charakterisieren sich die Lecythidaceae als eine sehr homogene und gut definierte Familie, die sich durch die folgenden Eigenschaften auszeichnet 1) Fibrose Struktur, hervorgerufen durch die Fasern, aus denen sich der Hartbast ausschliesslich zusammensetzt. 2) Lamellse, geschichtete Struktur infolge der Anordnunq des Hartbastes in Form von dnnen kurzen Lamellen, die stufenweise bereinander geschichtet sind. 3) Bildung gerader und feiner, wenn auch mehrreihiger Markstrahlen. 4) Karo-Musterung infolge der besonderen Anordnung des Hartbastes und der ihn senkrecht schneidenden Markstrahlen. 5) Fehlen eines Dilatationswachstums (mit zwei Ausnahmen). 6) Fehlen von Steinzellen (mit einer Ausnahme). 7) Hufige Bildung einer geschichteten Felodermis. 8) Gelegentliche Bildung eines geschichteten Korks. 9) Vlliges Fehlen eines sekretorischen Systems. 10) Bildung U-frmiger Membranen in der Peridermis. 11) Gewhnliches Fehlen einer deutlich unterschiedenen usseren Rinde. 12) Bildung von Ringelborke neben Schuppenborke. Die Schichtstruktur des Phloems frdert (und provoziert geradezu) die Bildung einer Ringelborke. 13) Die Schichtung herrscht als Musterbildung in den meisten Geweben der Rinde vor. 14) Die regelmssige Struktur der Rinde legt den Gedanken nahe, dass es sich hier um einen hochentwickelten und forgeschrittenen Typ im phylogenetischen Sinne handelt.

Wood anatomy of 14 species of the genus Pouteria Aubl. (Sapotaceae) growing in Venezuela was studied. The following species were studied: P. amygdalicarpa, P. caimito, P. coriacea, P. cuspidata subsp. dura, P. decorticans, P. egregia, P. eugeniifolia, P. guianensis, P. hispida, P. macrophylla, P. procera, P. reticulata, P. trilocularis and P. venosa. Wood description was done according IAWA Committee list. An one way ANOVA and Tukey test for multiple comparisons was performed regarding quantitative features. Secondary xylem shows homogeneity in Pouteria genus; the main distinctive features between species are pore diameter, pit diameter, rays width and number of wide cells in parenchyma bands. According to these features, a dichotomous key was elaborated. Pouteria decorticans and P. hispida can only be separated using quantitative features like diameter of intervessel pits. Similar case was observed between P. egregia and P. procera, separated by fibre length.
41740985|La biologia reproductiva de 17 especies de Melastomataceae fue estudiada en la Gran Sabana (estado Bolivar, Venezuela) mediante cruces controlados en el campo; se determin el ndice polen/vulo, la asignacin de biomasa floral y la eficiencia reproductiva naturai para cada especie y su relacin con el sistema reproductivo. La agamospermia (tres especies (17,7%) agamospermas y seis (35,3%) facultativas) fue el sistema reproductivo predominante, seguida por la autocompatibilidad (siete especies, 41,2%) y slo Tococa guianensis es autoincompatible. La mayoria de las especies estudiadas presentaron alta relacin polen/vulo, lo cual no se corresponde con sistemas agamospermos de reproduccin. La biomasa floral revel que la especie autoincompatible tiene la mayor relacin de biomasa androceo/biomasa de gineceo, lo que concuerda con la hiptesis de asignacin de biomasa. Sin embargo, los patrones de asignacin de biomasa en los otros sistemas reproductivos no mostraron tendencias claras. La produccin de frutos fue altamente variable e independiente del sistema reproductivo; no obstante, todas las especies autocompatibles mostraron bajos niveles de produccin de frutos y la especie autoincompatible tuvo alto valor de produccin de frutos por flor. The reproductive biology of 17 species of Melastomataceae was studied in the Gran Sabana plateau (Bolvar State, Venezuela) by means controlled crossings in the field; the pollen/ovule ratio, the allocation of floral biomass and the natural reproductive efficiency for each species and its relation with the breeding system were estimated. Agamospermy (three species (17.7%) and six (35.3%) facultatives) was the reproductive system, followed by self-compatibility (seven species, 41.2%), and only Tococa guianensis was selfincompatible. Most of the studied species displayed high pollen/ovule ratio, which does not correspond with agamospermous reproductive systems. Floral biomass revealed that the selfincompatible species has the greater androecium/gynoecium biomass ratio, which agrees with the hypothesis of biomass allocation. Nevertheless the patterns of biomass allocation in the other reproductive systems did not show clear tendencies. Fruit production was highly variable and independent of the reproductive system; however, all selfcompatible species showed low levels of fruit production and the selfincompatible species display high fruit production.

The floristic composition of four environments in La Palmita swamp, Zulia State, Venezuela was studied: inlet, sandy bar, mangrove forest and ecotone. Sampling (n = 16) was bimonthly, from October 2007 to May 2008, in both rainy and dry seasons, and done in a waterland (west-east) direction. Forty-eight species, 43 genera and 32 families were identified, including 17 trees, seven shrubs, 14 grasses, three hemiparasites, and seven vines. The ecotone area comprised "salinas" and halophytic grass communities. Salinity values suggested a low-high gradient (from 3,9  0,8 to 20,6  2,3 ppm) from inlet to ecotone zone. This study contributes to the knowledge of the estuarine wetland flora of the region.

41740674|Las especies estudiadas de Mimosaceae forman un grupo homogneo, pero no muy destacado de otras familias, ya que no muestran muchas especialidades. La corteza es algo parecida a la de las Sapotaceas por la agrupacin de las fibras en forma de placas cortas alternantes y por la ordenacin de las clulas secretoras en forma de hileras tangenciales. Los gneros Inga y Pithecellobium forman grupos homogneos dentro de las Mimosaceae y se aparecen en muchas caractersticas. De inters especial es el sber estratificado, sea en forma de capas alternantes suberificadas y no suberificadas o sea en forma de estratos de clulas cortas alternantes con estratos de clulas alargadas radialmente. Las lenticelas estratificadas se consideran como formas precursoras del corcho estratificado. Un sber estratificado de dimensiones enormes se encontr en el Samn, donde las hileras de clulas alargadas se separan una de otras longitudinalmente para formar grandes espacios intercelulares; de esta manera se origina un aernquima. La estratificacin del corcho viene de procesos rtmicos de actividad meristemtica (en las capas de clulas cortas) y de diferenciacin (en las capas de clulas alargadas). El ritidoma escamoso del Samn puede alcanzar una anchura 4 veces mayor del tejido cortical restante; no es solamente el ritidoma ms ancho de todas las Mimosaceae, sino tambin de todas las especies estudiadas en la Guayana Venezolana. Otra caracterstica de la corteza de las Mimosaceae es el sber dentado. Adems se pudo distinguir una corteza de juventud de una de vejez. The species studied of Mimosaceae represent a homogeneous group, but do not differ very much from other families, as they do not show many special characteristics. The cortex is somewhat similar to that of the Sapotaceae because of the arrangement of the fibers in the form of short alternating plates and of the secretory cells is the form of tangentially enlarged rows. The genera Inga and Pithecellobium form homogeneous groups within the Mimosaceae and resemble each other in many characteristics. Of special interest is the stratified cork, be it in the form of alternating suberized and not suberized layers or in the form of layers of short cells alternating with layers of radially elongated cells. The stratified lenticels are considered precursory forms of the stratified cork. A stratified cork of enormous dimensions occurs in the Saman, where the rows of radially enlarged cells separate longitudinally from each other in order to from large intercellular spaces; in this way, an aerenchyma arises. The stratification of the cork is explained by rhythmic processes of meristematic activity (in the layers of short cells), on the one hand, and by processes of differentiation (in the layers of enlarged cells), on the other hand. The rhytidome of the Saman can reach a width 4 times larger than that of the remaining cortical tissue; it represents not only the thickest rhytidome of all Mimosaceae studied, but also of all the species studied in the humid forest of Venezuelan Guayana. An other speciality of the cortex of Mimosaceae is the dentated cork. Furthermore, a juvenile form of the cortex can be distinguished from an aged one.

41740878|Una revisin preliminar de Polygalaceae en el subcontinente indio ha sido preparada sobre la base de la observacin de diferentes especies pertenecientes a esta familia en un hbitat natural y el anlisis de especimenes de nerbano y de literatura taxonmica. En el subcontinente indio (Bangladesh, Bhutan, Myanmar, Nepal, Pakistan, Sri Lanka e India) la familia Polygalaceae est pobremente representada (6,37% de la distribucin global). Este artculo trata la distribucin, fitoendemismo, posibles fsiles ancestrales, potencial econmico y riesgos de supervivencia de especies existentes. El estado actual de fitoendemismo en Polygalaceae en el subcontinente indio (35 ,29% en 2002-2007) ha sido comparado con la informacin de investigaciones anteriores (21,87% en 1939-1940) fnalizadas en el sigio XX. El aumento de la tasa de endemismo indica un incremento en el numero de especies endmicas un lapso de decrecimiento de especies pan-endmicas pertenecientes a esta familia. Para una mejor comprensin de los aspectos funcionales del porcentaje dinamico de las especies, la tasa de endemismo de un grupo determinado ha sido usada aqui corno un indicador clave. El crecimiento en una misma zona geogrfica ha sido registrado en intervalos de tiempo diferente y posteriormente es considerado para narrar los estudios acadmicos en la forma de presupuestos economicos de recursos renovables para asegurar su conservacin y uso sostenible. A preliminary checklist of Polygalaceae in Indian subcontinent has been prepared on the basis of primary observations of different taxa belonging to this family in wild habitats and on secondary observations based on examined herbarium specimens and taxonomic literature. On the Indian subcontinent (comprising Bangladesh, Bhutan, Myanmar, Nepal, Pakistan, Sri Lanka and India), the family Polygalaceae is poorly represented (6.37% of global distribution). The present paper deals with a brief review of distribution, phytoendemism, possible fossil ancestry, economic potential and survival threat on existing taxa. The present status of phytoendemism of Polygalaceae in Indian subcontinent (35.29% in 2002-2007) has been compared to the data of previous investigations (21.87% in 1939-1940) done in the XX century. The increasing rate of endemism either indicates towards increasing number of endemic taxa or decreasing span of distribution of pan-endemic taxa belonging to this family. For a better understanding of the functional aspects of species dynamics the percentage of rate of endemism of a particular group of plants has been used as key index here. The growing on same geographical location has been recorded in different time intervals and has further been considered to narrate the academic studies in form of qualitative economic appraisal of renewable resources for ensuring its conservation sustainable utilization.

Esta especie se identific como Rhodogorgon ramosissima J.N. Norris & Bucher, constituyndose en un nuevo registro para la costa venezolana. During a survey of the phycoflora of Morrocoy National Park, located on the western coast of Venezuela, samples of a red algae (Rhodophyta) resembling a gorgonian, which was growing on dead corals a 6 m depth, in Cayo Pescadores was collected. This pink algae has a 25-30 cm long leathery, and slick thallus with irregular branching, greasy consistancy and impregnated with mucilage. The thallus in cross section is characterized by a medular region with many interwoven and ramified filaments of 3-4 m in diameter. The tips of these filaments are branched at the upper end and were bulbous due to a terminal calcite-sheathed cell. The species was identified as Rhodogorgon ramosissima J.N. Norris & Bucher. This is the first report of this algae in Venezuelan coasts.
41740546|La idea central del presente trabajo es proponer la utilizacin de caracteres reproductivos en la seleccin de especies de plantas para la recuperacin de reas degradadas. El diseo de esta investigatin est basado en el concepto de la aptitud biolgica de las especies, la cual resulta del producto de la reproductin y la sobrevivencia de las especies. De acuerdo a este concepto se utilizan 16 caractres reproductivos y 4 caractres ecolgicos, con la finalidad de encontrar especies de plantas con: 1. amplia dispersabilidad natural, 2. baja susceptibilidad a enemigos naturales en etapas de semillas y en estado adulto, 3. elevada y permanente productin de semillas, 4. un sistema de apareamiento que promueva una baja expresin de caractres deletreos, 5. morfologa floral que permita recibir una alta diversidad de visitantes florales, 6. polinizadores generalistas, ubicuos y predecibles y 7. mecanismos de dispersin de disporas que le permitan a las especies una diseminacin en las areas de ocupacin e inmigraciones de poblaciones distantes. Los mtodos propuestos y el significado de 20 caracteres son mostrados en detalle. Cada uno de los caracteres es tabulado como 0, 1 y 2, dependiendo de su importancia en promover la reproduccin. Se recomienda la escogencia de aquellas especies que acumulen 2/3 (65%) del total de la puntuacin mxima para experimentar en la recuperacin de reas degradadas. The central idea of this research is to use reproductive traits in selection of plant species for the restoration of degraded areas. The design of this investigation is based on the biological fitness concept, which is a result of reproduction and survivorship. According to this concept, ecological and reproductive characters (20) were used to detect plant species with: 1. broad natural dispersion, 2. low susceptibility to natural enemies in seed and adult stages, 3. high and permanent seed production, 4. a mating system that promotes low expression of deleterious characters, 5. a floral morphology that allows to receive a large diversity of floral visitors, 6. generalist, predictible, and ubiquitous pollinators, and 7. dispersal syndromes of diaspores with capacity to recolonize areas and/or the eventual immigration from distant populations. Methods and meaning of the 20 characters used are shown in detail. For each character, the state of the characters was considered as 0,1 y 2, depending of their value in promote reproductive success. Plant species are selected on the basis of the cumulative points. Those species with 2/3 (65%) or more of the total points are recommended for further experimental studies in habitat restoration.

41740990|Se analizaron las relaciones entre caracteres reproductivos, diversidad de visitantes florales (DVF) y frecuencia de visitas (FV), en 30 asterceas simptricas del bosque chaqueo de Crdoba (Argentina). Tanto la DVF como la FV fueron muy diferentes entre las especies, siendo Apis mellifera el insecto que realiz comparativamente la mayor cantidad de visitas. La DVF y la FV mostraron correlaciones significativas negativas con la duracin de la floracin y positivas con el nmero de flores abiertas por planta. Los resultados sugieren que el aseguramiento reproductivo que proporciona la autopolinizacin espontnea seri limitado, puesto que la actividad de los polinizadores tiene un papel relevante en la reproduccin. Tanto en estas especies como en las que no son capaces de producir frutos por autopolinizacin espontnea, se incrementaron el nmero y el tamao de los frutos producidos por polinizacin natural. The diversity of floral visitors (DFV) and the frequency of visits (FV) were related to some reproductive traits, in 30 co-occurring Asteraceae species of Chaco forests from Crdoba (Argentina). DFV and FV were very different between species ana Apis mellifera was the most frequent visitor of flowers. The DFV and the FV showed significant correlations: negative with flowering period and positive with the number of open flowers per plant. Results suggest that the reproductive assurance by autonomous selfing may be limited, since pollinator activity plays an important role in plant reproduction. Both, species with and without autonomous selfing, showed an increase in the number and size of the fruits produced.

El rea considerada est ubicada en el oeste del pais, representa la ramificacin oriental de la Cordillera Oriental de Colombia, abarcando los Estados Tchira, Mrida, Trujillo y Lara, as corno la zona limitrofe (piedemonte andino-llanero) de los Estados Barinas y Portuguesa con la Cordillera de Mrida y la depresin del Estado Tchira. Based on the results of numerous botanical explorations made in the area of the Cordillera of Mrida in Venezuela, on the examination of an extensive series of herbarium specimens, and upon the review of literature, this paper presents a discussion on the diversity and distribution of the genera and species of the Solanaceae family in the Cordillera of Mrida. This area is located in the western part of the country and represents an extension of the branch of the Eastern Cordillera of Colombia; it includes Tchira, Mrida, Trujillo and Lara states, as well as the adjacent Andean piedmont in Barinas and Portuguesa states with the Cordillera of Mrida and the depression of Tachira state. The Cordillera of Mrida constitutes an important center of diversity and endemicity with floristic affinities with the Caribbean and Guayana regions of Venezuela, as well as the Eastern Cordillera of Colombia. Because of the floristic richness of this cordillera, it is necessary to increase the phytogeographic knowledge of its forests, referring to the distribution of the diversity and endemics.

Se discute la variabilidad cariotipica interespecifica en funcin de posibles reordenamientos cromosmicos. Chromosome characteristics from five Aloe species were compared. The karyological observations were carried out from root tips treated with colchicine and following traditional procedures. ANOVA, DMS mean tests and euclidean distances, based on chromosome size, length of the arms (1 and s) and ratio r (1/s), showed interspecific significant differences and clustering between A. arborescens and A. succotrina, followed by A. vera and separation of A. chinensis and A. saponaria as apart group. Moreover, differences for karyotypic asymmetry, number and position of secondary constrictions were observed. Karyotype variability among species from possible chromosomal rearrangements was discussed.
41740824|El presente artculo relata el proceso de construccin del Herbario Nacional de Venezuela hasta la muerte de su fundador, el botnico norteamericano de origen suizo Henri Pittier (1857-1950). The paper shows the building of the Venezuelan National Herbarium till the death of its founder, the American Botanist born in Switzerland Henri Pittier (1857-1950). It present, through the correspondence that Henri Pittier had with officials and colleagues, local and foreign, the struggle and the loneliness a man of science can find when trying to build a scientific oriented institution in a hostile or unfriendly environment to this kind of enterprise.
